# wiki/index.md — catalog

Read this before loading any individual page. Load pages selectively.

The wiki is split into two strata:

- `base/` — **stratum 0**: prior knowledge and human-anchored resources. Source of truth about human semantics.
- `findings/` — **strata above**: this project's own typed work.

[`meaning-senses.md`](meaning-senses.md) is the controlled vocabulary every findings page must tag against.

This page is the **project entry point**: start here to read the project's status and decide what to do next. The dashboard immediately below is the decision-relevant view; the full typed-page catalog follows under [Pages](#pages).

---

## Status & next steps — start here

### What to do next
- [`executive-summary.md`](executive-summary.md) — plain-language summary of the project's purpose and current state (refreshed each session); read this first for orientation.
- [`NEXT.md`](../NEXT.md) — current state and the next concrete action / fan-out backlog.
- [`log.md`](../log.md) — dated history of every run.
- Current synthesis: [`findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md) — the live theory page (evidence ladder + where each finding sits).
- Relational-axis synthesis: [`findings/theory/relational-meaning-in-llms.md`](findings/theory/relational-meaning-in-llms.md) — the "second ladder" arc consolidated (reference-game null, coined-term reassignment order-sensitivity positive, perturbation v2–v4 text-position, order-composition C-series); a **thin-positive / floor-characterizing** arc — order-effects are real but model-internal/transcript-recoverable, constitution is not reached (rich rung structurally out of reach for text-only probes).
- Philosophical-map synthesis: [`findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md`](findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md) — positions all findings on the classical map of meaning (where, if anywhere, LLM meaning lives; what each finding supports / strains / is silent on).

### Open decisions
These gate promotion of contingent findings; nothing depending on them is settled until ratified. **Since 2026-06-12 ratification is autonomous and cross-session** (an independent adversarial-review pass in a *later* session than the one that opened the decision — see [`PROTOCOL.md`](../PROTOCOL.md) §2 and [`decisions/resolved/autonomous-era-governance`](decisions/resolved/autonomous-era-governance.md)); a `resolution:` block or file-move from Tom still outranks everything.

Forty-seven decisions have been ratified to date (full per-decision changelog: [`decisions/resolved/index.md`](decisions/resolved/index.md)). The most recent — the **vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity** question (a VALID recovery-scoring rule for the NL-baseline adequacy audit, so the competence band is applied to a valid measurement) — was **ratified 2026-06-28 (session 128, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 127, ratified session 128; the boundary held): ADOPT Q-A WITH MODIFICATIONS** ([`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity.md) — replace the invalid deterministic literal-target-word-lemma scorer with a held-out **two-judge category-match re-grade** of the stored auditor guesses, **cross-only** (each held-out judge grades the *other* auditor's guesses), judged against the human gold `{word, phrase}` under a strict semantic-referent-identity instruction in which literal string overlap is declared insufficient-and-irrelevant, with mandatory per-item (a) word-referent / (b) recovered-referent / (c) verdict fields so every string-overlap rubber-stamp is hand-auditable; metric = two-judge mean high-recovery; band `[0.60, 0.95]` CONFIRMED FIXED; the re-grade owes its **own** fresh pre-run-critic GO before the IMAGE arm is read). The prior most recent — the **vwsd-nlbaseline-audit-params** operationalization question (the three deferred numbers of the NL-baseline adequacy audit) — was **ratified 2026-06-28 (session 127, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 126, ratified session 127; the boundary held): ADOPT-DEFAULTS as a slate** ([`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-audit-params`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-audit-params.md) — **P1** graded none/partial/high recovery, band metric = high-recovery rate (mirrors v2's .130 high-leak rate; the tilt-prone exact-gold option rejected); **P2** author = panel.A claude-sonnet-4.6, two held-out auditors panel.B gpt-5.4-mini + panel.C gemini-3.5-flash, band on the two-auditor mean (the author-identity coupling is legitimate, not scope-creep; the two-auditor mean answers the parent's single-vs-multiple circularity flag); **P3** band `[0.60, 0.95]` (lower edge ~4.6× the de-referented .130 floor, upper edge the symmetric oracle guard); anti-cheat + quote-integrity PASS; both edges bracket channel competence only, never the residual width). **No decision is currently open.** The one decision open at this session's start — [`decisions/resolved/monotonicity-cancel-arm-redesign`](decisions/resolved/monotonicity-cancel-arm-redesign.md) (opened session 135) — was **ratified 2026-06-28 (session 136, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened s135, ratified s136; the boundary held): ADOPT C1 (telic-completion) conditional on its own B2 calibration, C2 (privative) fallback, then a principled-limit closure if both fail, MODS M1–M3.** It asked how to re-design the cancel arm of the monotonicity-generalization battery after its ratified *for*-durative/semelfactive "only once" cancel arm hit a **B2 ceiling-gate NO-GO** when s135 built and ran the gate ([`result/monotonicity-generalization-b2-nogo-v1`](findings/results/monotonicity-generalization-b2-nogo-v1.md)): the add arm passes cleanly (construction 1.00 / control 0.00, 3/3 models) but the cancel default ("only once") floors at 0.00 in 3/3 models under both instruments — single-occurrence is a defeasible implicature, not a lexical entailment, so it cannot reach the matched ceiling under strict NLI. The failure is **structural** (not verb-selection), so the cancel coercion needs a re-design (a yardstick change → cross-session); the spend-bearing asymmetry was **not run** and never read; the conjecture stays `proposed`. The ratified verdict makes the provisional default binding-with-a-condition: run C1's completion-default B2 calibration **first** (NO-GO → C2 after a written conjecture-scope amendment; a second NO-GO → principled-limit closure); the re-designed cancel arm must itself clear a fresh B2 default-at-ceiling gate before any asymmetry is read. The add arm, B2 machinery, and frozen thresholds are retained unchanged. — The decision open at this session's *start* (now resolved) — [`decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization.md), **ratified 2026-06-28 (session 134, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened s131, prereq (1) discharged s133, prereqs 2–4 supplied + ratified s134; producing sessions excluded as sole ratifier): ADOPT-WITH-MODS** — was the operationalization gate for the matched-difficulty add-vs-cancel **generalization test** of [`conjecture/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry`](findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md): **(a)** WHICH new add-vs-cancel construction pair(s) the battery uses (beyond the existing caused-motion/way [add] vs conative [cancel]), and **(b)** the matched-difficulty / ceiling certification criterion (so the comparison is at matched task structure, not add-at-ceiling vs cancel-off-ceiling — mirroring how [`result/conative-cancel-direction-v2`](findings/results/conative-cancel-direction-v2.md) was certified). Ratified yardstick: a **single new-pair `internal-contrast-only` leg** — **ADD = resultative** (verified headroom-clean pool; trap verbs `freeze`/`sharpen` excluded) vs **CANCEL = the *for*-durative aspectual (semelfactive-iteration) coercion** (a genuinely new pair) — certified by B1+B2 with frozen numbers (add licensing-no-cue ≥ 0.80 & bare control ≤ 0.40 & cancel default ≥ 0.80 in ≥2/3 models on a calibration subset, else re-pair before spend; asymmetry read at a 20 pp margin; instrument-fragility at ≥10 pp), with three hygiene mods (disjoint cancel pool — `kick`/`bounce` removed; dedupe; the contestable "only once" default gated by B2). A3's anchored-replication leg was **dropped** (prereq 4: [`result/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md) already covers the anchored base, which "is not the matched-difficulty test"). Surfaced by the scoping page [`open-question/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-design`](findings/open-questions/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-design.md). Named failure mode (tuning the pair/bar until the asymmetry appears) guarded by freeze-and-hash + an independent pre-run-critic GO/NO-GO. **History:** s132 KEEP-OPEN (four prerequisites recorded) → s133 discharged prerequisite (1), the load-bearing add-arm-headroom blocker, via a frozen, pre-run-critic-GO'd, post-run-verified calibration probe ([`result/addarm-headroom-calibration-v1`](findings/results/addarm-headroom-calibration-v1.md); both candidate add constructions demonstrate headroom — resultative 10/12 verbs clean, construction affirm 1.000 vs control 0.250) → s134 supplied prerequisites 2–4 and an independent fresh-agent review ratified (ADOPT-WITH-MODS). Fixes the yardstick, never the result: the conjecture stays `proposed` and the spend-bearing battery is **not** run in the ratifying session — a later session freezes-and-hashes the resultative-add + *for*-durative-cancel item set, runs the B2 blocking gate, gets a fresh pre-run-critic GO, and runs the matched battery with the falsify arms live. — Otherwise, no decision carried over from prior sessions is open. The one decision open at the session-128 start — [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity.md) — was **ratified this session (session 128, autonomous adversarial review; ADOPT Q-A WITH MODIFICATIONS)** and moved to resolved/ (see the most-recent entry above). It had been surfaced by the **s127 NL-baseline magnitude run's pre-run-critic NO-GO**: the run was built and frozen (1158 fluent NL descriptions, the TEXT-NL arm not saturated, the held-out adequacy audit run), but the audit landed **OUT OF BAND** (two-auditor mean high-recovery **0.342** < the `[0.60, 0.95]` floor) — and an independent critic verified this is a **scorer-validity artifact, not a degenerate channel**: the ratified deterministic scorer counts "high" only on the **literal target-word lemma**, but VWSD target words are mostly technical/Latinate/spelling-variant/proper-noun forms a competent description names by common name (~64/70 "none" items are faithful category recoveries mis-scored — the v2 design-B.4 gap). The magnitude read is **deferred, the IMAGE arm was NOT read** ([`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1.md)); this decision proposes a **valid recovery-scoring rule** (default Q-A: a held-out model re-grade of *category match* using the stored raw guesses, per B.4) so the band is applied to a valid measurement. All frozen artifacts are reusable verbatim — the re-attempt owes a cross-session-ratified re-grade + a fresh critic GO, **no re-authoring spend**. The just-closed decision — [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-audit-params`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-audit-params.md) (opened session 126, **ratified 2026-06-28, session 127, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — the boundary held: ADOPT-DEFAULTS as a slate**) — pinned the **three numbers the ratified competence-standard *shape* deferred to the run session**: the held-out **recovery-scoring rule** (P1: graded none/partial/high, band on the high-recovery rate), the **held-out audit model(s) + coupled author identity** (P2: author = panel.A claude-sonnet-4.6; auditors = panel.B gpt-5.4-mini + panel.C gemini-3.5-flash, both held out from the author, band on the two-auditor mean), and the two-sided **band edges** (P3: `[0.60, 0.95]` on the high-recovery rate, grounded on v2's de-referented `.130` incompetence floor). Ratifying fixed the yardstick before any NL description was authored (anti-cheat: the band is set before authoring, never tuned to land a narrow-or-wide result); the band gates **channel admissibility only, never the residual-width result** (both narrow and wide first-class). The prior decision — the **vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv** gate ([`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv.md), opened session 122) — *what standard of "competence" must the VWSD natural-language candidate description meet, so the residual-width magnitude read is a property of ordinary language and not of an over- or under-competent captioner?* — was **ratified 2026-06-27 (session 123, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 122, ratified session 123; the boundary held): ADOPT-DEFAULT (Q1-C)**. It surfaced the value-laden core of the natural-language-baseline magnitude follow-up the v2 result owes (its Limitation 1): a two-sided failure (an **oracle** channel → artificially **narrow** residual, the mirror of v2's manufactured headroom; a **degenerate-weak** channel → artificially **wide** residual, v2's own failure re-imported). Of three options (Q1-A reuse v1's saturating captions; Q1-B fresh fluent descriptions under a fixed policy; **Q1-C = Q1-B + a held-out adequacy audit with a pre-registered two-sided target band**), the reviewer adopted **Q1-C** — the only option that *empirically pins* the channel between the two artifacts — confirming the circularity worry is acknowledged-and-bounded (v2's own held-out leak audit already discriminated on this dataset) and deferring the numeric band edges, the audit model, and the recovery-scoring rule to the run session. This fixes the **yardstick, never the result**: [`design/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline`](../experiments/designs/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline.md) is now cleared to be **frozen** under the standard, but `result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline` stays gated by a fresh pre-run-critic GO + a cap-clearing pre-flight before any run. — The single decision open at the session-114 start — the **prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes** cost-optimization question ([`decisions/resolved/prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes`](decisions/resolved/prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes.md), opened session 113, Tom-directed) — was **ratified 2026-06-26 (session 114, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened s113, ratified s114; the boundary held): ADOPT THE DEFAULT unchanged** — leave the probe harness on the cold-read path; gate any caching behind a $0-stakes matched cold-vs-cached pilot (byte-identical outputs + measured saving) before adoption; code-checked that `billed_cost()` keeps the **recorded** figure correct (it sums the API's `usage.cost`) while the `RATE_CARD` pre-flight estimate would *over-count* a cached run; **no result depends on it** (a cost optimization, not a correctness gate; harnesses UNCHANGED). The **prior** decision open at a session start — the **v2 non-caption-baseline** gate for a VWSD grounding-headroom probe ([`decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv-v2`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv-v2.md), opened session 104) — was **ratified 2026-06-25 (session 105, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 104, ratified session 105; the boundary held): ADOPT-DEFAULT** (Q1 Option B sense-neutral visual-form descriptor as the separability baseline + Option-A chance-floor calibration arm + Option-C leakage-audit covariate; Q2 stratified draw clearing a re-stated per-stratum floor, covariate frozen per-model pre-image, day-split if over cap; Q3 v1's narrow human-anchored posture unchanged; binding conditions a–f incl. new (d) raised claude image-arm `max_tokens` — all as written; quote-integrity + anti-cheat PASS). It fixes the **yardstick, never any result**: the conjecture [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) stays `proposed`, and a build session is now **cleared to author** `design/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2` under the resolved gate (Option-B descriptors + leak-audit frozen and checksummed; stratified draw clearing the floor; per-model covariate frozen pre-image; raised claude `max_tokens`) — still gated by a fresh pre-run critic GO + a fresh-UTC-day budget before `result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2` can run. — The session-92 anchor question — may the [`resource/semeval2017-pun-corpus`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md) serve as the sense-co-activation anchor for the forced-both lexical line — was **ratified session 93 (2026-06-23, ADOPT DEFAULTS)**: [`decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns`](decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns.md) adopts the corpus as the **Q4 co-activation** anchor (Q-A), keeps a **separate dominance step** owed for Q1-ii (Q-B-1, co-presence ≠ no-dominance), and admits **attested homographic puns** as forced-both stimuli (Q-C-1, homonym subset, sha256-frozen). The forced-both line is thereby unblocked for a future build (still gated by a fresh pre-run critic + budget; the fork stays at **R1** until that build runs). — A prior resolved decision — [`decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization.md) — was **OPENED session 89 (2026-06-23) and RATIFIED session 90 (2026-06-23; ADOPT DEFAULTS; the cross-session boundary held)**. It operationalizes the **discriminating test** named by [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md): how to build and score a **genuinely-unresolvable (forced-both) lexical item** — a pun / zeugma / co-activated double-entendre — so a probe can separate **(A) layer-specialness** (the word-sense layer always draws a pick) from **(B) always-resolvability** (the models commit wherever a reading is pickable, and word-sense has only ever presented pickable items). Four questions, all **adopted at default**: **Q1-iii** certify forced-both vs a *leaning* homonym (zeugma/co-predication structural frame **+** an independent balance check, frozen) — the hard part, where the essay's expected trigger-(c) "cannot cleanly certify" lives, and the reviewer confirmed the gate **fails safe** (an uncertifiable item is *declared uncertified*, not let through); **Q2-i** a **forced-single-application** instrument on which "it means both" is structurally *not* a dodge; **Q3** a sha256-frozen reading rule inheriting the sibling gates' C1/C3/C4, with `answer-both` kept as its own class and **commit** (the burden-discharging surprise for A) held to a *higher* anti-cheat bar; **Q4** anchor `internal-contrast-only` unless a sense-**co-activation** resource is separately cross-session ratified (no anchor invented). The deflationary **(B)** holds the burden; the run stays gated by a future independent **pre-run critic GO/NO-GO** + budget, and **trigger (c)** ("cannot cleanly certify", fork stays at R1) is the honest expected first outcome. **The build was attempted session 91 (2026-06-23) → trigger (c) FIRED** ([`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md), VERDICT-SOUND on independent review): Q1-i + Q2-i + Q3 are buildable, but **Q1-ii (the independent not-model-based balance check) is not satisfiable** under no-human-subjects (only a barred human annotator or forbidden model output could certify the constructed sentence's balance; SemCor general-usage balance is both too sparse — 1/8 powered — and the wrong measure), so no model ran ($0) and the fork stays at R1 until a sense-co-activation / in-item-balance resource is found + separately ratified. — The prior decision, the matched-ambiguity-kind gate ([`decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level`](decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level.md), opened session 85), was **ratified 2026-06-22 (session 86; ADOPT DEFAULT — see Resolved decisions below)**: Q1 Option B (keep DWUG; *add* a balanced-homonym disjunctive lexical class as a *within-lexical* scalar-vs-disjunctive contrast, level held fixed) + Q2 anchor **`internal-contrast-only`** for the disjunctive arm unless a future homonym sense-resource is separately ratified + a binding **nuisance-matching freeze** (register/length/frequency/syntactic-frame between the two lexical classes). The **within-lexical scalar-vs-disjunctive probe was built, frozen, pre-run-critic-GO'd, and RAN (session 87) → SURVIVAL 3/3** ([`result/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1`](findings/results/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1.md)): on a genuinely-disjunctive balanced homonym (no tie-break) all three models **commit** (near-zero UNCLEAR) exactly as on a scalar bridging midpoint, level held fixed → the lexical commit-without-hedging is **not** an artifact of the softer scalar stimulus; [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md)'s "kind, not level" reading **dissolves at R2 for the lexical case** (its trigger (b) FIRED — a first-class positive about the word-sense layer, with one disclosed residual: a balanced homonym is still resolvable-by-committing where a relational dual-binding is not). The shared-instrument gate (opened session 80) was **ratified session 82 (2026-06-22; ADOPT DEFAULT — see Resolved decisions below)**, promoting its contingent [`conjecture/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment`](findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md) `proposed → designed → tested`: the shared-instrument cross-level probe **RAN (session 84) → DISSOLUTION (3/3 models)** — the graded-aggregate/discrete-moment shape does **not** survive instrument-equalization ([`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md)); the deflationary "three rhyming facts" default stands. (Separately, the lexical bridging-context probe [`findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md`](findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md) remains buildable under its two resolved gates + a fresh pre-run critic; the function-word probe's count-vs-matching blocker was resolved earlier; build-v2 of [`findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md) runs under its resolved decision.)

The prior decision, `function-word-anchor-design` (opened session 65), was **ratified 2026-06-21, session 66 (autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — the boundary held): ADOPT WITH MODIFICATIONS** → [`decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design`](decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design.md): SUBTLEX-US ([`base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md)) as the Q1 frequency-matching floor (|ΔLg10WF| ≤ 0.10 + length/predictability, frozen+hashed before any output); entailment-flip / forced-choice the sole confirm/falsify-bearing indicator; `internal-contrast-only` posture with an optional non-blocking BLiMP/NLI upgrade.

### Resolved decisions
Forty-six decisions have been ratified to date (the full per-decision changelog with rationale now lives in [`decisions/resolved/index.md`](decisions/resolved/index.md), moved there 2026-06-18 to keep this always-loaded index lean — decision [`decisions/resolved/wiki-frontmatter-ergonomics`](decisions/resolved/wiki-frontmatter-ergonomics.md)). Ratified by Tom through 2026-06-12; thereafter by the autonomous cross-session procedure (each page records its `resolved-by`). Ratifying an anchor/operationalization fixes the *yardstick*, not the *result*.
- **Most recent:** the **constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization** gate — the yardstick for the matched-difficulty add-vs-cancel **generalization** battery of [`conjecture/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry`](findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md) — *ratified 2026-06-28 (session 134, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened s131, prereq (1) discharged s133, prereqs 2–4 supplied + ratified s134; producing sessions excluded as sole ratifier): **ADOPT-WITH-MODS*** ([`decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization.md)). Fixes a single new-pair `internal-contrast-only` leg — **ADD = resultative** vs **CANCEL = the *for*-durative aspectual (semelfactive-iteration) coercion** — certified by B1+B2 with frozen numbers (add no-cue ≥ 0.80 & bare control ≤ 0.40 & cancel default ≥ 0.80 in ≥2/3 models, else re-pair; 20 pp asymmetry margin; ≥10 pp instrument-fragility); A3's anchored-replication leg **dropped** (prereq 4); three hygiene mods (disjoint cancel verb pool — `kick`/`bounce` removed; dedupe; the contestable "only once" default gated by B2). Fixes the yardstick, never the result: the conjecture stays `proposed`; the spend-bearing battery is **not** run by the ratifying session. The prior most recent — the **prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes** cost-optimization question, *ratified 2026-06-26 (session 114, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 113, ratified session 114; the boundary held)*: [`decisions/resolved/prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes`](decisions/resolved/prompt-caching-repeated-prefix-probes.md) — ***ADOPT THE DEFAULT unchanged***. A Tom-directed (s113) question of whether to use OpenRouter prompt caching on repeated-prefix probes (cached input reads ~10× cheaper) to cut input cost. A fresh independent reviewer adopted the provisional default as written: **keep the probe harness on the cold-read path** ([`experiments/lib/openrouter.py`](../experiments/lib/openrouter.py) UNCHANGED); before adopting caching, run a **$0-stakes matched cold-vs-cached pilot** that confirms byte-identical outputs and measures the actual saving + input-token share; adopt only where the saving is material and output-neutral (implicit-caching gemini/gpt first, Anthropic `cache_control` only if its measured share justifies it); if the saving is small (the **expected gemini case** — output+reasoning at $9/MT dominate, caching touches only input), record the **null** and retire the lever; if adopted, add a cache-aware term to the `RATE_CARD` estimate. **Code-check PASS:** `billed_cost()` sums the API-returned `usage.cost` (cache line items already folded in → recorded figure stays correct automatically); `RATE_CARD`/`estimated_cost()` model only `(prompt, completion)`, so a cached run would be **over-estimated** until the term is added. **Anti-cheat PASS:** not result-motivated (no current or planned result depends on this — a cost optimization, not a correctness gate), and the default *strengthens* both cost-accounting correctness and design reproducibility. Yardstick fixed, never any result. `contingent-artifacts: []` — nothing promoted/retired; the pilot it authorizes is optional follow-on work. No probe ran, no spend. Logged in [`log.md`](../log.md).
- **Prior most recent (forced-both lexical):** the **forced-both-lexical-operationalization** gate, *ratified 2026-06-23 (session 90, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 89, ratified session 90; the boundary held)*: [`decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization.md) — ***ADOPT DEFAULTS***. Fixes the yardstick for the **discriminating test** that would separate **(A) layer-specialness** from **(B) always-resolvability** for the surviving lexical commit ([`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md)): how to build + score a **genuinely-unresolvable (forced-both) lexical item** (pun/zeugma/co-activated double-entendre). A fresh independent reviewer adopted all four defaults — **Q1-iii** (zeugma/co-predication frame **+** an independent, not-model-based balance check, both sha256-frozen; the reviewer confirmed it **fails safe** — an item that cannot be certified independent of model output is *declared uncertified*, never let through), **Q2-i** (a **forced-single-application** task on which "it means both" is structurally unavailable, dissolving the unfalsifiability trap at the instrument level), **Q3** (sha256-frozen reading rule; `answer-both` kept as its own class; **commit held to a HIGHER anti-cheat bar** + a clean-subset check; C1/C3/C4 inherited from the sibling gates), **Q4** (`internal-contrast-only` unless a sense-**co-activation** resource is separately cross-session ratified — a *stronger* human-grounding demand than the balanced-homonym class, and DWUG "does not tag pairs as polysemy vs. homonymy", so no anchor is invented). **Quote-integrity PASS** (load-bearing quotes verified character-for-character against the essay, the two result pages, [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) and [`resource/dwug-usage-graphs`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md)); **anti-cheat PASS** (every default makes a spurious (A) win *harder*; the "cannot cleanly certify" NULL is first-class; verdict **not** result-motivated). No probe ran, no spend; the run stays gated by a future pre-run critic GO/NO-GO + budget, with **trigger (c)** ("cannot cleanly certify", fork stays R1) the honest expected first outcome. `contingent-artifacts` empty (the essay is `contingent-on: []`, held at R1, unaffected); nothing promoted/retired. Logged in [`log.md`](../log.md).
- **Prior most recent:** the **matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level** gate, *ratified 2026-06-22 (session 86, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 85, ratified session 86; the boundary held)*: [`decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level`](decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level.md) — ***ADOPT DEFAULT + one added binding condition***. Fixes the yardstick for the follow-up that would separate "the lexical level is special as a model fact" from "a usage-similarity midpoint is a *softer* ambiguity than a structural one" — the comparability residual the cross-level dissolution disclosed. **Q1 = Option B** (keep the human-anchored DWUG scalar-bridging lexical leg; **add** a balanced-homonym **disjunctive** lexical class as a *within-lexical* scalar-vs-disjunctive contrast, **level held fixed**) over Option A (full cross-level matched-kind, held in reserve — needs a reachable Q2-a homonym sense-anchor) and Option C (defer as "unresolvable at this N" — refuted by B being a concrete freezable design). **Q2 = Q2-b (`internal-contrast-only`)** for the new disjunctive arm unless a sense-annotated homonym resource is separately cross-session ratified (no anchor invented; verified against [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) that DWUG "does not tag pairs as polysemy vs. homonymy"); weakest-common-strength floors the disjunctive arm. **Q3** instrument + C1–C4 inherited unchanged and re-frozen; matched-kind certification + item ids + survival/collapse threshold sha256-frozen before the first probe; survival (which would partly revive the defeated unified conjecture) held to a *higher* bar, reported symmetrically with collapse. **Added binding condition — the nuisance-matching freeze:** the two lexical classes matched (or stratified/controlled) on register/token-length/frequency-band/syntactic-frame before any model call, residual imbalance disclosed and led with. **Anti-cheat PASS** (B varies only the KIND with the level fixed → cannot smuggle a softer stimulus to manufacture a survival; the freeze forecloses re-selecting the class against model confidence; the reviewer spot-checked the two result quotes + the cap quote verbatim and confirmed the verdict is not result-motivated). No probe ran, no spend; the run stays gated by a future pre-run critic GO/NO-GO + budget. `contingent-artifacts` empty (the essay [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) is `contingent-on: []`, held at R1, unaffected). - **Prior most recent (2):** the **cross-level shared-instrument-operationalization** gate, *ratified 2026-06-22 (session 82, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened session 80, reviewed-and-strengthened session 81, ratified session 82; the boundary held)*: [`decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/cross-level-shared-instrument-operationalization.md) — ***ADOPT DEFAULT***. Fixes the yardstick for a **shared-instrument cross-level probe** (one commitment instrument applied identically at the lexical/constructional/relational legs, frozen + sha256'd before any result, per-level instrument-shopping forbidden of the "aggregate/moment" shape): **Option A** (explicit graded "unsure/both/unclear" + 0–100 confidence) with **four binding build-session conditions C1–C4** — (C1) categorical **decline**, not confidence, load-bearing for the moment pole at every level; (C2) numeric/wording/per-level-definition **sha256 freeze**; (C3) per-level clear-class precondition → **NO-GO**; (C4) a confidence shift without a decline shift is a **self-report effect, not graded-moment evidence**. The reviewer verified C1/C4 verbatim against the two lexical result pages. Anti-cheat PASS (every condition makes a spurious *positive* harder; the dissolution NULL stays first-class; no probe ran, no spend). Logged in [`log.md`](../log.md).
- **Prior most recent (3):** the **lexical bridging-context** gates, both *ratified 2026-06-21 (session 75, autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened by session 74, ratified by session 75; the boundary held)*. [`decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-operationalization.md) — ***ADOPT DEFAULT + 3 binding mods***: a fixed **B-primary (graded confidence) + C-categorical-cross-check ("both/unclear")** panel, **A characterizing-only**; reading rule is **per-axis** (position by B alone; confidence/dispersion by both B and C), **not** a blanket B–C AND; **numeric freeze + sha256** of bands/wording before data; **B–C disagreement is a mixed/weak result, not the null**; v1 clause-(c) context control bound non-optional. [`decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-anchor`](decisions/resolved/lexical-bridging-context-anchor.md) — ***ADOPT design with a CLAIM-SCOPE CAP***: the **DWUG-derived bridging stratum** (within-period DURel 2–3 / high-disagreement, **≥3-rater floor**) + WiC clear poles, but the **human-comparison claim is capped to *usage-similarity* intermediacy** (never "two senses co-present"); **collapses to `internal-contrast-only`** if the floored bridging pool is too thin to power the 3-class contrast; one quote-integrity correction applied at integration. Both fix the *yardstick, never the result* (no probe ran); contingent artifact [`findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md`](findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md) is now **buildable**. Logged in [`log.md`](../log.md).
- The prior most recent: [`decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching`](decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching.md) — *ratified 2026-06-21 (autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened by session 67, ratified by session 68): **ADOPT A DIFFERENT OPTION — provisional default OVERTURNED***. The function-word probe's ≥200-item-count-vs-faithful-matching tension. The reviewer re-derived the crux and found the relax-length default unsound: the function arm is **degenerate in Δlen** (every function swap is +1 char → Δlen ≡ +1, zero variance, perfectly collinear with condition), so length **cannot be regressed/stratified out** — stratifying collapses to the build-v1 set, regressing identifies the contrast only off the +1 stratum, so the "restored" Δ0 routes never enter the bearing contrast. Length stays a **hard freeze-time gate** (per-pair signed-Δlen equality). Adopted: **widen the function-word inventory** (Option E's add-pairs half, frequency tolerance UNCHANGED at |ΔLg10WF| ≤ 0.10) + capped Option-A carrier-authoring; **fix the freq-only-reader residual build-v1 actually failed** (the v1 record overstated soundness — it failed three certification checks: count, ≥4-class span, and the freq-only reader 0.1212 > 0.12); the **≥200/≥4-class bar UNCHANGED** (Option D rejected as goalpost-moving). Anti-cheat PASS (the overturn makes a spurious positive harder; the reviewer declined the easier path because it is unsound, not to change a result; boundary held). Contingent artifact: [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md) stays `designed`; build-v2 runs under nine binding conditions + a fresh pre-run critic. Logged in [`log.md`](../log.md).
- [`decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design`](decisions/resolved/function-word-anchor-design.md) — *ratified 2026-06-21 (autonomous adversarial review, cross-session — opened by session 65, ratified by session 66): **ADOPT WITH MODIFICATIONS***. Fixes the yardstick for the **function-word-vs-content-word swap** probe ([`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md)). **Q1** SUBTLEX-US ([`base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md), fetched + sha256-pinned this session) as the frequency floor: content controls within |ΔLg10WF| ≤ 0.10 + length(±1)/predictability, pair-level where feasible (will→would) and condition-level with mirrored spread where not (because→although 1.41, some→every 0.50), the set frozen+hashed before any output. **Q2** entailment-flip / forced-choice the sole confirm/weak/falsify indicator (the dead-KL prediction-1 demoted to a secondary characterizing-only proxy — M1, conjecture amended); a binding manipulation-check (M3). **Q3** `internal-contrast-only` posture; the BLiMP/NLI human backing an optional fetch-first upgrade that never blocks the within-model run. The reviewer confirmed every joint makes a spurious positive *harder* (single norm removes norm-shopping; freeze+hash removes post-hoc re-selection) and the falsify arm (content-swap shift ≥ function-swap shift = a clean positive for the distributional camp) stays live. Conjecture → `designed`; a build session must still construct + certify the frozen set before any spend.
- The next most recent was [`decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator`](decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator.md) (*ratified 2026-06-20 (cross-session, sessions 49→50): **ADOPT MODIFIED***; corpus production surface as primary anchor, graded forced-choice indicator, synthetic minimal pairs with a numeric length↔givenness dissociation control, four modifications + seven binding build conditions); before it [`decisions/resolved/wiki-frontmatter-ergonomics`](decisions/resolved/wiki-frontmatter-ergonomics.md) (ratified 2026-06-18) and the 27 earlier ratifications — see the [history page](decisions/resolved/index.md).
