- [`findings/essays/instrument-corrects-the-hand-read.md`](findings/essays/instrument-corrects-the-hand-read.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-28, session 129); **"The instrument corrects the hand-read"** (philosophical / methodological track). Crystallizes the **session-127 → session-128 VWSD NL-baseline** episode into a *point about the epistemics of estimation*: where a **probe-able instrument can be built**, a careful **adversarial hand-read** — even a sharp reviewer's quantified eyeball (the s127 critic's "~64 of the ~70 'none' items are faithful category recoveries") — systematically **over-credits**, and is not a substitute for a **frozen, held-out, strict-rubric instrument**; the in-repo case shows the divergence was **decision-relevant** (the eyeball put the channel above the 0.60 floor, the two-judge category-match instrument put it at **0.438, below**), and a fresh critic verified the lower number **valid in both directions** (κ 0.608), so the correction was real, not a new artifact. Two corollaries: (i) build the instrument *even after* a smart reviewer has already looked — "a smart person already looked" is the condition under which skipping is most tempting and here would have been wrong; (ii) the **two-sided band did the hard half of its job** — it partly rescued the over-harsh literal scorer (0.342→0.438) *and then held the line* on a substantive below-floor read (deferring a channel that does not clear the floor even after the scorer artifact was removed). Explicitly **distinct** from [`essay/audit-brackets-instrument-competence`](findings/essays/audit-brackets-instrument-competence.md) (that essay *designs* the band; this one is the epistemics *once the band exists*), [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) (sampling *jitter* of one method vs. *systematic over-credit bias* of a different, cheaper method), [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) (borrows no validity-theory machinery), and [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (symmetric magnitude correction, not an asymmetric can't-claim). **No new empirical claim, no human comparison** (both source results are `internal-contrast-only`; the magnitude read is un-run); the lesson is a **conjecture-from-one-case**, not a proven law (5 revision triggers). `depends-on` [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-regrade-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-regrade-v1.md) + [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1.md); `refines` [`essay/audit-brackets-instrument-competence`](findings/essays/audit-brackets-instrument-competence.md) + [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md). (created 2026-06-28; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/two-topics-language-as-object.md`](findings/essays/two-topics-language-as-object.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-28, session 128); **"Two topics, one model"** (philosophical track). Lifts **Lewis 1970**'s methodological split — the description of a language as an **abstract semantic object** (a function from expressions to meanings) vs. the **psychological-and-sociological use-facts** whereby one such object is the language a population actually *uses* — and applies it to "does an LLM *have* a language." Original move: the project's behavioral method is a **topic-one instrument** (it measures the expression→behavior mapping) that can succeed completely while **topic two** (is there a population/convention/common-knowledge selecting this as the language the model *uses*?) stays untouched and separately owed; the project's positive findings cluster on topic one and its two hardest silences — **reference** and **relational constitution** — are revealed as topic-two (selection-fact) silences, and reading topic two off topic-one systematicity is named as the specific LLM-form of Lewis's error. Flags a live equivocation: the *operational* "convention" of the relational pages (a latest-binding rule in the mapping) is not Lewis's *metasemantic* convention (the population-selecting fact). A **distinction-tool, not a measurement** — adjudicates neither topic; the payoff is precision about a principled limit. Explicitly distinct from (and `refines`) [`theory/situating-llm-meaning`](findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md) (re-describes the map's "model-internal positive / referential-and-relational silent" pattern as a topic-one/topic-two split), and sits *upstream* of [`essay/reference-as-premise-bound`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md), [`essay/inherited-not-constituted`](findings/essays/inherited-not-constituted.md), [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md) (supplies the frame onto which their silences sort, not their specific results). One Lewis passage quoted verbatim (truth-conditions, pp. 22–23); the two-topics framing itself is the source page's *characterization* of Lewis, not a verbatim quotation (revision trigger (a) armed for the Lewis *Convention* primary). Four revision triggers. **No new empirical claim** (every empirical/textual assertion cites its in-repo page verbatim); `depends-on` [`source/lewis-1970-general-semantics`](base/sources/lewis-1970-general-semantics.md) + the three relevant concept pages. (created 2026-06-28; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/audit-brackets-instrument-competence.md`](findings/essays/audit-brackets-instrument-competence.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-27, session 123); **"One audit, two directions"** (grounding axis / philosophical track). A *measurement-epistemics* point about **magnitude reads**: when a behavioral probe measures a **size** (how *wide* a residual is) rather than a **direction/shape** (does X gate Y at all), the dominant uncertainty is often not the model but the **instrument's own competence** — a single authored description channel's competence level silently *sets* the magnitude — so the honest move is not to *assert* the channel competent (by policy/intent) but to **bracket** its competence empirically between its two **symmetric failure modes** (an over-competent oracle → artificially **narrow**; an under-competent degenerate → artificially **wide**) via a held-out recovery audit read against a **pre-registered two-sided band**. Second, concrete contribution (the genuinely-new sliver): **the same held-out-recovery device guards opposite artifacts in successive designs** — a *leak* audit in [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md) (bar a channel revealing **too much**; high-leak .130, Spearman .160, discriminative not vacuous) becomes a two-sided *adequacy* audit in the NL-baseline successor (bar a channel revealing **too little** *or* too much). Grounded in the v1(saturated)→v2(manufactured)→NL(audited-middle) symmetry and the [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv.md) gate ratified this session (Q1-C). Explicitly **distinct** from [`essay/headroom-positive-vindicates-the-null`](findings/essays/headroom-positive-vindicates-the-null.md) (that essay is about *what a result means*; this is about *what a magnitude instrument must do to be trustworthy*, and starts where that one stops — "shape, not size"), [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) (sampling *jitter*; here the bias is *systematic*, unremovable by re-running), [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (*asymmetric* can't-claims; here the two artifacts are *symmetric* by construction), and [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) (no validity-theory machinery borrowed). Bounded to `grounded.perceptual`/`referential.sense` on binary VWSD gold; **no** human comparison beyond it; **no new empirical claim**, ratifies nothing, the magnitude verdict is **un-run**. Five revision triggers (the band turning out **empty/un-hittable** on VWSD → evidence the bracketing strategy fails for this axis; an unaudited magnitude accepted in-repo; the leak→adequacy duality failing to generalize; a clean narrow-under-band read; the band defeated by shared training distributions). `depends-on` v2 + the NL-baseline design + the s122 essay; `refines` [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md). (created 2026-06-27; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/headroom-positive-vindicates-the-null.md`](findings/essays/headroom-positive-vindicates-the-null.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-27, session 122); **"A positive that vindicates a negative"** (grounding axis / philosophical track). Its original contribution is a second-order **epistemic interlock**: a null on a *structural variable* can under-determine **its own interpretation** until the matched-regime positive arrives, so the positive is partly **constitutive** of what the negatives were evidence for. Applied to the grounding axis — three nulls + one inconclusive run — whose session-121 [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md) cell is its **first confirming direction**: the positive discriminates **(a) modality-inert** from **(b) text-saturated** (a fork the conjecture flagged but the nulls alone could not close) and picks **(b)** — the prior nulls were measuring *saturation*, not *inertness*. The rigor spine: the positive licenses the gating **SHAPE**, **not** the **SIZE** (the magnitude is instrument-inflated by the de-referented channel, Limitation 1 quoted verbatim), so the narrow-vs-wide-residue question stays open and is exactly what the owed natural-language-baseline test settles. Explicitly distinct from [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (forbids upgrading a null to a *can't*-claim) and [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) (a single number's run-to-run jitter). Bounded to `grounded.perceptual`/`referential.sense` — behavior *sensitive to* the word→sense→image mapping in the residual, **not** reference, **not** a perceptual symbol system; **no** human comparison beyond the VWSD binary gold; v2 honesty discounts (gemini floor, gpt sign-only/degrades, manufactured magnitude) carried. Five revision triggers (the magnitude test returning narrow / wide; a failed v2 replication; a graded-image resource; the gpt anti-grounding signal hardening). `depends-on` v2 + the two nulls + v1 + gradience + the conjecture + undischargeable-negative; `refines` [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md). **No new empirical claim.** (created 2026-06-27; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-22; **trigger (b) FIRED session 84** — the cross-level shape dissolved at R2 in [`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md), the anticipated worked example of a rhyme correctly *not* promoted to a mechanism); "**From rhyme to mechanism**" — a reusable **evidence standard** (a graded *convergence ladder*: **R0** shared vocabulary → **R1** native-instrument agreement → **R2** instrument-equalized → **R3** break-test survival → **R-ceiling** mechanistic identity, named out-of-reach for a behavioral project) for when a cross-level / cross-instrument **family resemblance** may be upgraded to a **single-mechanism** claim. The rule: assert a cross-level unification **only at the rung the evidence has reached**; below R2 it stays a *rhyme*, filed as an open-question, never a finding. The **symmetric twin** of [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (you can't prove "one mechanism" from rhyme, as you can't prove "M cannot" from behavior); break-test logic from [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md); explicitly **distinct** from the construction evidence-ladder (one-mechanism-vs-rhyme, not meaning-vs-form). `refines` the OQ; `supports` [`conjecture/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment`](findings/conjectures/cross-level-gradience-aggregate-not-moment.md). - [`findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 87 — **trigger (b) FIRED: the central reading DISSOLVED at R2 for the lexical case**, [`result/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1`](findings/results/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1.md) returned **SURVIVAL 3/3** — the models commit on a balanced homonym too, so the lexical specialness is the **word-sense layer, not the scalar-vs-disjunctive kind**; the kind-reading is retracted for the lexical case [kept visible], the conceptual scalar/disjunctive contrast survives, one residual bounds "layer" [a balanced homonym is still resolvable-by-committing]); originally **draft** (2026-06-22, session 85); **"Kind, not level"** — a **re-reading** of the cross-level dissolution ([`result/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1`](findings/results/cross-level-shared-instrument-v1.md)). Argues the dissolution's commit/decline split is more parsimoniously indexed by the **kind** of indeterminacy than by the **level**: the models *commit* on a **scalar** ambiguity (a graded similarity with a *nearer pole* to lean to — the lexical bridging stimulus) and *decline* on a **disjunctive** one (two complete readings/bindings, *both/neither*, no nearer pole — the constructional/relational items), so the lexical leg's specialness may be the **softness of its stimulus, not the word-sense layer**. Explicitly **does NOT revive** the dissolved level-conjecture: kind is confounded with level in that design, so the kind-reading is held at **R1** on the [`convergence ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md), *not* asserted as a finding, and routed to the matched-ambiguity-kind probe ([`decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level`](decisions/resolved/matched-ambiguity-kind-cross-level.md), **ratified session 86 → the within-lexical probe is now buildable**). The discriminating test: a *disjunctively*-ambiguous lexical item (balanced homonym, no tie-break) should draw decline, not commitment, if kind (not layer) drives the split. `refines` the OQ; `depends-on` the result, the dissolved conjecture, the ladder, the three level-home essays, [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-22; **philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 91 — **trigger (c) FIRED**: the discriminating probe was *attempted* under the resolved gate and **terminated at certification** — Q1-ii, the independent not-model-based balance check, is not satisfiable under no-human-subjects; fork **stays at R1**, no model run, $0 → [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md), VERDICT-SOUND on independent review); originally **draft** (2026-06-23, session 88); the successor to (and `refines`) [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md), written the same session 87's SURVIVAL result landed it. Takes the **load-bearing residual (caveat 1)** of [`result/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1`](findings/results/within-lexical-scalar-vs-disjunctive-v1.md) and forks the *surviving* lexical commit into two rival readings: **(A) layer-specialness** (the word-sense layer always draws a discrete pick, whatever the kind/structure of ambiguity) vs **(B) always-resolvability** (the models commit wherever a reading is *pickable*, and word-sense has only ever presented pickable items — so the lexical leg looks special only because its ambiguities stay resolvable). Shows the SURVIVAL design **cannot separate** them (a balanced homonym is *both* lexical *and* resolvable, so both readings predict commit), and names the one stimulus that would — a **genuinely-unresolvable lexical item** (a forced-both pun / zeugma, the lexical analogue of the relational same-round **dual binding**), with the **asymmetric prediction**: commit under (A), decline under (B). Leads with the honest certification difficulty (the "it means both" third response makes the verdict an artifact of the scoring rule unless the instrument asks a *forced-single-application* question). Bridges to [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)'s **single-reader-recoverability** criterion (reading (B) = lexical ambiguities stay on the *thin/recoverable* side; the bridge is the *criterion*, not the constitution metaphysics) and to [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) (B predicts a lexical genuine-both with no distributional tie-break draws **abstention**). Held at **R1** on the [`convergence ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md), with the **deflationary (B) holding the burden**. `refines` [`essay/ambiguity-kind-not-level`](findings/essays/ambiguity-kind-not-level.md) + [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md); `depends-on` the two results, the ladder, transcript-ceiling, [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison; the discriminating probe has not run.** The R2-rung operationalization the essay named — how to build + score a forced-both lexical item — was **ratified session 90 (2026-06-23, ADOPT DEFAULTS)**: [`decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/forced-both-lexical-operationalization.md), so a forced-both probe is now **buildable under the resolved gate + a fresh pre-run critic** (the essay stays at R1, unaffected; trigger (c) "cannot cleanly certify" the honest expected first outcome). (created 2026-06-23; **lexical / philosophical track**)

- [`findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md`](findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-14; draft→revised when the v6 replication landed); **the project's THIRD essay** (grammatical / philosophical track). Argues, from the AANN inferential **v4 PARTIAL — now replicated cell-for-cell by [`result/aann-inferential-v6`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v6.md) across two disjoint item sets** — that a forced-choice paraphrase *preference* and an NLI entailment *commitment* are evidence for **two different constructs** — graded **distributional compatibility** (a use/family-resemblance probe) vs. defeasible **inferential commitment** (a truth-conditional / inferentialist probe) — **not** two noisy readings of one latent "use." Where they dissociate (v4/v6: the construction shifts paraphrase preference in all three models but carries to NLI + the agreement reflex in only gpt-5.4-mini — the "largest forced-choice-vs-NLI disagreement in the project's record", and **off-ceiling**, so genuine divergence not compression), "does the model *use* the construction's meaning?" has **no single model-level answer**: "use" decomposes into a preference component (present panel-wide) and a commitment component (present in one model). Maps FC→Wittgensteinian use-pole, NLI→truth-conditional pole — the two semantic theories pulling apart inside one model's behavior — and draws the consequence that the evidence ladder's **top two rungs can come apart**, which v4/v6 instance. Companion to (and `refines`) the second essay: that one is about the question being *unreachable* (v3 ceiling); this one about it being *reachable but the instruments disagreeing*. `internal-contrast-only`; explicit revision triggers — **(a) powered NLI convergence for claude/gemini → retract for them, and (b) FC shift failing to replicate → thesis weakens were both EXERCISED by v6 and NEITHER fired** (claude/gemini NLI still did not converge; the FC shift did replicate), so the essay was *strengthened*, not retracted; a human anchor entering would still revisit the caveat. **2026-06-15 scope-limiting datum (no trigger fired):** the first attempt to generalize the dissociation to a different construction came back negative ([`result/conative-preference-commitment-v1`](findings/results/conative-preference-commitment-v1.md), INCONCLUSIVE) — bounding the essay's instanced scope to AANN (the two-constructs *type* point stands; any *general-ordering* reading is contradicted by data). (**grammatical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/inference-default-coincidence.md`](findings/essays/inference-default-coincidence.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-13); **the project's SECOND essay** (grammatical / philosophical track). Argues one bounded *methodological* thesis from the AANN inferential v3 ceiling-bounded null: for a next-token model, a construction's **licensed inference can be behaviorally indistinguishable from the phrase's distributional default**, and where the two **coincide** a shift-from-control design cannot reach the inferential question at all — "the default eats the construction." Names the **two compounding limits** (can't-say-like-humans = `internal-contrast-only`; can't-separate-from-the-default = the coincidence) and draws the evidence-ladder consequence: the top rung (inferential *use*) may be **unreachable by within-model contrast for exactly the constructions whose contributed reading is most entrenched as a default** — a selection effect, not a verdict on the models. Joins this to the lexicon–grammar continuum as the **grammatical-side analogue** of the lexical/multimodal saturation (text already carries the distinction). The lone v3 positive — gpt-5.4-mini's singular-agreement reflex — sharpens, not undercuts, the thesis (it moved precisely where the default points the *other* way). Rests entirely on the `internal-contrast-only` v3 result; no human-comparison claim, no resource anchor owed. (**grammatical / philosophical track**)

- [`findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-15, triggers (d)+(e) fired); **the project's SIXTH essay** (referential / philosophical track). Argues the in-repo dispute over whether an LLM's words **refer** (word-to-world) is **premise-bound, not evidence-bound**: [`base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md`](base/sources/mandelkern-linzen-2024-do-words-refer.md) and the project's own [`base/concepts/referential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) run the **same** externalist (Putnam/Kripke) metasemantics to **opposite** verdicts, disagreeing only on the antecedent of M&L's §4.3 community-membership conditional ("*If* they are part of a linguistic community … then their use … refers") — a fact fixed **off-board** (by natural history, not any in-head/in-behavior fact), so **no behavioral probe the project can run adjudicates it**. The original contribution is the **structural diagnosis**: this is a cell of the meaning map where the project's behavioral method is *constitutively* silent — a principled limit, not a gap more probes can close. Draws **two citation-discipline consequences**: (1) don't cite the grounding nulls as bearing against reference (history-channel vs perception-channel orthogonality); (2) don't cite M&L as *establishing* reference (its verdict is modal/premise-conditional) — cite it only as making the concept page's in-principle "no" *contestable*. Stays descriptivist; ranks neither pole. Distinct from the relational essays (word-to-world axis + a premise *no probe reaches*, vs. the relational axis + a *null a probe produced*). The central thesis is **unchanged and better-instanced**: all three published parties argue by *conceptual* means and **none adduces a measurement**, which is premise-bound-not-evidence-bound exhibited by the disputants' own practice — Ostertag even frames his disagreement as turning on an antecedent he doubts, not the conditional he accepts. New trigger (f): a published voice claiming a *measurement* settles LM reference would directly challenge the thesis. (**referential / philosophical track**)

- [`findings/essays/stereotype-without-the-expert.md`](findings/essays/stereotype-without-the-expert.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-25, session 110); a **referential / philosophical-track** essay, the third in the reference cluster (sibling of the sixth and seventh), and the first to build on the freshly-ingested [`base/sources/putnam-1975-meaning-of-meaning.md`](base/sources/putnam-1975-meaning-of-meaning.md). Original contribution, a **tripartite component-and-role mapping**: it pulls Putnam's account of a natural-kind term into its three separable components — the **stereotype**, the indexically-fixed **extension** (`sameL`, p. 152), and the role-structured **division of linguistic labor** (p. 144-146) — and maps the LLM onto each. The map is **lopsided**: the model has **maximal** access to component (1), the *stereotype* ("a standardized description of features … typical … stereotypical," p. 147) — which Putnam isolated as precisely the component that does **not** fix extension; **no** access to component (2), the indexical tie to locally-sampled stuff (the concept page's "no 'Twin Earth' to move it to"); and — the sharp point — it occupies **neither role** in component (3): not the *deferring layperson* (no expert behind it) and not the *anchoring expert* (no recognitional method, no stuff), while having ingested that structure's **pooled output**. Payoff (modest): the project's measured distributional success reads, in the referential frame, as **stereotype-competence** — exactly what Putnam predicts a stereotype-bearer to have, and exactly the component his account says does not by itself reach reference (**"the elm/beech speaker writ large"**). **`refines`** [`findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md) by sharpening its "is the model in the community?" antecedent into a "which role?" question (answered: *neither*) **without settling it**; distinct from [`findings/essays/reference-denials-disunified.md`](findings/essays/reference-denials-disunified.md) (a positive component-mapping, not a denial-anatomy). **No new empirical claim, no number, no human-comparison;** conditional on the externalist frame; the "distributional training ≈ stereotype-extraction" identification flagged as the essay's own analogy, not a measured fact. `depends-on` [`base/sources/putnam-1975-meaning-of-meaning.md`](base/sources/putnam-1975-meaning-of-meaning.md) + [`base/concepts/referential-meaning.md`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) + [`base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). (created 2026-06-25; **referential / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-17 draft; **2026-06-17 trigger (a) fired → rung (ii) occupied**; **2026-06-18** Option-C made composition order-sensitive, occupied by claude only under a forced format + rung (iii) rich side documented structurally closed for text; **2026-06-19** the stricter thin rung is now **panel-concordant given a working surface** across two non-commuting pairs [D4, A4] — superseding the one-model reading as a forced-format/output-channel artifact, still THIN); **the project's EIGHTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), built on the "order-sensitive but thin" relational positive ([`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md)). Its contribution is **conceptual, not empirical**: it builds the structure [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) said was missing — a **four-rung ladder** above the relational bottom ((i) order-sensitive *overwrite* = latest-binding-wins; (ii) order-sensitive *integration* / non-overwrite repair; (iii) *path-dependence* proper / live-vs-shuffled; (iv) genuine *between-agent constitution* / Brandomian scorekeeping), each with a candidate behavioral signature and a discriminating design — plus a sharp **single-reader-recoverability criterion** cutting thin (updated) from rich (constituted): a convention is *thin* if its recovered interpretation is computable by any single reader from the record's content+stamps, *rich* only if recovery requires a surplus no single reader could reconstruct. Rungs (iii)–(iv) stay *unbuilt*; the instrument **cannot separate rung (i)/(ii) from (iii)** (the claim's scope limit 3); the firm thin floor makes the *distance* to constitution measurable and large. **No human comparison** (cited results `internal-contrast-only`). - [`findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) — status: **live** (2026-06-17 draft; **promoted to live 2026-06-18** — its named puncture test, revision trigger (a), was run in a *later* session ([`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md), the strongest order-load-bearing text design buildable) and did **not** fire: the pre-run gate ruled the operation-order gap THIN, corroborating the ceiling. `live` = an active standing position, **not** proven; all four triggers stay live, (a) for *other* Option-C designs); **the project's NINTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), the cross-cutting successor to (and `refines`) the eighth. Defends, as a **conjecture about the project's own method** (hedged throughout, not a proof): the cut tracks the **record itself**, so a text-only probe is **structurally ceilinged at the thin side** — it can show updating, integration, even non-commuting operations, but the rich-side surplus (a live two-party normative trajectory; arrival-order not encoded in the final state) is constitutively *not in any transcript*. - [`findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md`](findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's TENTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), the **constructive complement** to the ninth ([`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)). Where the ceiling essay argues *text cannot* reach the rich side, this one asks, forward, what an instrument that *could* reach **rung (iv)** (genuine between-agent constitution) would have to be — and answers: **a scored live practice, not a transcript.** Its defining requirement is a class of observables that exist only between parties and only while the interaction is live — Brandomian deontic scorekeeping (characterized-not-read in-repo via [`concept/inferential-meaning`](base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md)): at minimum **commitment undertaken vs merely uttered** (answerability), **entitlement granted/withheld by the other party**, and **a challenge and whether it was discharged** — each a *status instituted by uptake*, hence a surplus no single reader of a record can reconstruct, so recording it requires a live two-party practice, not a depiction (extends the ceiling essay's chess-scoresheet image to "a refereed game in progress"). Holds a key **discipline: rung (iii) ≠ rung (iv)** — a non-text medium that merely carries arrival-order surplus would bound the transcript ceiling (rung iii) but is *strictly weaker* than recording normative status (rung iv). Explicitly **builds nothing, measures nothing, promises nothing**: the instrument is a requirement-specification the project may never construct (no in-repo human dyadic resource with normative observables; Clark & Wilkes-Gibbs 1986 unfetched and scoped to collaborative reference, not scorekeeping). **No human comparison**; quotes no Brandom directly. Names exactly the event the ceiling essay's revision trigger (b) anticipates. `refines` [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/capability-split.md`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's ELEVENTH essay** (relational / philosophical track), a **methodological** unit prompted by Option C being the **first relational rung to split the panel** ([`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md): claude RESPECTS-ORDER at ceiling, gemini UNINTERPRETABLE). Its original contribution is a **reporting discipline**, not an empirical claim: a one-model (split) positive is **not** a property of "the models"/"LLMs" but a **capability split** attributable only to the model that showed it. Rungs (i)–(ii) read as "both panel models" *because the panel happened to concord* — concordance is contingent, not a safe default. A split licenses only a per-model **existential** (claude composes two non-commuting moves at ceiling, with transparent reasoning) plus a per-model **negative** — and the negative here is an **instrument-capability limit, not a clean order-blind null** (the gate "correctly refuses to read" gemini's COMP rate; gemini cannot compose even on demand, DIRECT 0.583), so it must **not** be read as "gemini lacks order-sensitive composition in general." Standing recommendation: mark every panel verdict **CONCORDANT vs SPLIT**, never average a split into a panel-level claim (the project's past findings were *already careful* — this is forward discipline, not an accusation). Logs "claude > gemini" as a **thing to watch, not a finding** (refuses the cross-task extrapolation on one probe). **No human comparison.** **Trigger (b) tested 2026-06-18 → did NOT fire (no witness):** the easier K=4 re-run ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md)) halved the instrument and neither gemini (0.594) nor gpt (0.438) cleared the on-demand gate, so the split survives the easing — *strengthened*, not bounded to one instrument. **Tested a SECOND time (on-signature) 2026-06-18 → again no witness:** the figure-to-figure easing ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md)) removed the position↔figure read-off and neither gemini (0.656) nor gpt (0.250) cleared the gate; the single-move signature persisted (localizing the difficulty to chaining) → **figure-to-figure discharged**, trigger (b) live only for worked-example / fewer-steps. `refines` [`essay/update-is-not-constitution`](findings/essays/update-is-not-constitution.md); `depends-on` [`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md) + [`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18); **the project's TWELFTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **generalization** of the eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) and the ninth ([`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md)). Gives the charter's "write the null" discipline a **logical-epistemic backbone**: a capability *positive* is a **verifiable existential** (one witness — one elicitation on which the model succeeds — discharges it) while a capability *absence* ("M cannot do X") is an **unverifiable universal over elicitations** that no finite behavioral battery reaches — the **mirror** of the Popperian law/existence asymmetry, so from behavior alone the negative is **undischargeable**. This **vindicates** the null discipline rather than threatening it: the project's nulls are not capability-absence claims but instrument-relative facts, so writing them is honest and the only error is the silent upgrade to "M cannot." Builds a **typology of negatives** — (1) **effect-null under an instrument** (relational pilot's order-insensitivity; grounding redundancy), (2) **instrument-uninterpretable** / prerequisite-gate failure (gemini/gpt UNINTERPRETABLE on Option C), (3) **structural reach-closure** (the transcript ceiling — a negative about the *instrument's reach*, not the model's capacity) — and keeps a fourth box, a behavioral **capability-absence**, deliberately empty (only a non-behavioral architectural/mechanistic proof closes it; trigger (a)). Decision-relevant payoff: re-running a failing probe is futile (another ∀-instance, never the ∀); only a **witness-seeking** probe (an easier elicitation — exactly capability-split trigger (b)) or a structural argument can change a negative's status. Generalizes capability-split's clean-null/instrument-uninterpretable mark from the split-panel case to the single-model case, and lifts transcript-ceiling's structural closure into "kind 3." **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** `depends-on` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c.md) + [`result/relational-reference-game-v1`](findings/results/relational-reference-game-v1.md) + [`essay/rung-iv-instrument`](findings/essays/rung-iv-instrument.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-18; **deepened 2026-06-20, session 61** — the *partial-witness* slot, below); **the project's THIRTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the twelfth ([`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)). That essay proved a **witness-seeking** probe is the *only* behavioral move that can flip a capability-negative, but left open *how much* witness-seeking is worth — and since the elicitation space is open, "seek a witness" reads as unbounded against a finite budget ($5/day). This essay supplies the missing **economics of spending**. Its load-bearing move is the distinction between **logical closure** (a claim about the model — undischargeable from behavior, fully preserved) and **practical suspension** (a claim about the *project's spending* — provisional, reopenable, asserting nothing about the model); the project never *closes* a behavioral negative, it *suspends* the witness-search. The value of the next probe ≈ expected-info × P(fires) vs cost, where expected-info decomposes into **axis novelty** (easing the same axis twice has diminishing returns; a fresh axis is informative) and **signature match** (read the failure signature, ease the *implicated* axis — a non-witness from an off-signature easing is weak evidence). The highest-value terminator is a **structural bound** (a kind-3 reach-closure argument that retires a whole class of easings at zero spend — the transcript ceiling exemplifies it). Worked instance: the K=4 non-witness eased **one, off-signature** axis (track size, while the "single-move-reader" signature implicates *chaining*), which is exactly why [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) correctly keeps trigger (b) live and [`NEXT.md`](../NEXT.md) names a figure-to-figure / fewer-chaining-steps probe next. Adds a **witness-search suspension** reporting note (axes eased / implicated-but-un-eased / any structural bound / reopen condition), orthogonal to capability-split's CONCORDANT-SPLIT and undischargeable-negative's kind-1/2/3 marks; **never written as "M cannot."** **The named on-signature probe then ran ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md), 2026-06-18): no witness, the single-move signature persisting even under trivial-lookup moves — corroborating the off-signature reading of K=4, and the result page now carries the predicted suspension note (suspended on the read-off axis, not closed).** **Deepened 2026-06-20 (session 61) — the PARTIAL WITNESS:** session 60's let-alone forced-decomposition ([`result/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md)) returned a **third** outcome the fire/non-fire value model had no slot for — a *directional but underpowered* easing (gpt +0.21, p = 0.090, below baseline; "partially fired / candidate"), neither a clean fire nor a clean miss. The deepening adds the partial-witness slot and a **power-up scope clause**: its correct continuation is a **powered re-run of the same axis** (more items), which the "axis novelty / same axis twice" and parent-essay "more of the same probe cannot" cautions would wrongly forbid — the discriminator being **whether the first run produced a directional effect** (powering a *signal* resolves statistics, not the existence question a clean non-witness already answered); the exemption is narrow and self-extinguishing, and closure ≠ suspension is untouched (a partial witness keeps the search live). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** `refines` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md); `depends-on` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-easier-k4.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-figure-to-figure.md) + [`result/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md) + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-19); **the project's FOURTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the thirteenth ([`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md)). It **answers that essay's revision trigger (b)** — does a **structural bound** (kind-3 reach-closure) exist for *thin-side* two-move composition? — and answers it **in the negative; the negative is the contribution**. The composition witness-search is now suspended across **four** instruments with the structural bound recorded as "**none yet**" ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example.md) item (iii)); this essay asks whether the **≥2-move floor** (a composition needs ≥2 moves) plus the behavioral localization of the difficulty to "chaining execution" can be turned into a kind-3 bound, and shows it **cannot**, on three grounds: **(A)** the candidate bound's load-bearing premise ("the difficulty *is* the irreducible core") is a **behavioral universal** undischargeable per [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) — it is "M cannot chain" disguised as a structural argument (a **kind-4 smuggle**, refused); **(B)** the ≥2-move floor bounds only the *step-count* axis, leaving the elicitation space **open** along un-eased axes (a different/more-familiar non-commuting operation pair, execution-format scaffolding, many-shot); **(C)** — the **original contribution** — a **task-parameter floor** is the wrong *type* of object to be a reach-closure. The criterion: *a kind-3 reach-closure excludes the witness from an entire instrument **class** by a class-level (typically definitional, medium-level) property (the transcript ceiling: the rich-side surplus is constitutively absent from any record); a bound on a **task parameter** caps one knob and leaves the witness-bearing region (≥2 moves, open along other axes) populated — **not every floor is a ceiling.*** Verdict: **no kind-3 bound of the available type exists**, so the composition witness-search can only ever be **suspended on budget, never structurally closed** — upgrading the result's item-(iii) "none yet" from a placeholder to a **reasoned null**. **Sharpens** witness-seeking-economics (adds the gate a candidate bound must pass to count as structural) and **reinforces** the closure ≠ suspension line (guards against a parameter floor masquerading as a reach-closure). Leaves a **non-behavioral** capacity-closure open (undischargeable-negative trigger (a)). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` result read at strength). `refines` [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md); `depends-on` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-worked-example.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-19); **the project's FIFTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the twelfth ([`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)) and thirteenth ([`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md)), written off the 38th-session **witness** ([`result/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold.md)). Names a confound: the **output channel** through which a model must answer — a forced single token vs. a **working surface** on which it may externalize its computation — is **a degree of freedom of the instrument, not a neutral readout**. A channel too narrow to carry a multi-step computation can **mask** a capability the model has (the four-instrument composition split **dissolved** into panel-concordance when the channel alone was widened, reasoning-effort held constant); a wide channel can **scaffold** one. So there is **no neutral channel**, a behavioral capability claim is **indexed to a channel**, and an unindexed one is underspecified. Methodological upshots: a forced-format capability-**negative** is, until the channel is varied, **channel-bounded, never a capacity verdict** (the kind-2 verdict was a true measurement of a *channel-bounded* capability — the error the confound names is **mis-description**, not false measurement — preserving [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)); the channel is therefore a **mandatory, high-value control** the [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) allocation should rank among the **first** easings, not last (cheap; recurs across the instrument library; was the *decisive* axis here). **Scoped**: the confound bites only when the probed capability requires **serial, externalizable** computation **and** the channel forbids externalizing it — so single-token *tasks* (acceptability, single-premise NLI) are untouched. Draws a **machine performance/competence** map (the aperture is a performance constraint masking a competence — a frame, no human claim) and an **aperture-vs-ceiling dual** with [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) (input-medium ceiling vs. output-channel aperture; the two errors — ceiling-mistaken-for-aperture vs. aperture-mistaken-for-ceiling — are opposite ends of one instrument). Generalizes the single execution-format axis [`essay/floor-is-not-a-ceiling`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) objection (B) merely named. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` result read at strength). `refines` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md); `depends-on` [`essay/floor-is-not-a-ceiling`](findings/essays/floor-is-not-a-ceiling.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/transcript-ceiling`](findings/essays/transcript-ceiling.md) + [`result/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold`](findings/results/relational-order-composition-c-reasoning-scaffold.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-20; revision logged session 53 — the fresh-item replication [`result/dative-information-structure-v2`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v2.md) fired revision trigger (c) in the **strengthening** direction: the spread did NOT compress (gemini-to-gpt ≈9×→≈27×), gpt's v1 CONFIRM dropped to WEAK, so v1's concordant 3/3 demonstrably hid a fragile member — the essay's empirical spine is firmer, its discipline unchanged, the "wants replication" caveat discharged); **the project's SIXTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **refinement** of the eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) into the **concordant** case that essay left open ("*A concordant verdict may license a cautious panel-scoped sentence*"). Written off the session-51 dative result ([`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md)), the project's first human-anchored Tier-2 positive — a **CONCORDANT CONFIRM (3/3)** that nonetheless sits on an **order-of-magnitude effect-size spread** (gemini +0.524 ≫ claude +0.327 ≫ gpt +0.056, all clearing their bootstrap lower bound). Original contribution, a **reading discipline**: a binary panel verdict is a **threshold gate**, blind above the threshold, so the shared label "CONFIRM" can hide a wide magnitude spread; and because the dative conjecture's **prediction 3** (effect size *"decorrelates from surface accuracy"*) **confirmed**, the magnitude carries information the label discards. The fence: **a concordant verdict carries its spread** — report per-model magnitudes, mark them **tight vs decorrelated**, and read a wide-spread concordant CONFIRM as licensing the panel-scoped **direction/existence** sentence (*all three track X in the human direction*) but **not** a panel-scoped **magnitude/uniformity** sentence (*the models track X to a similar degree* / *at a rate of …*). Distinguishes **two textures of hidden heterogeneity** — magnitude decorrelation on one instrument (dative) vs across-instrument **convergence heterogeneity** (the AANN PARTIAL, via [`open-question/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md)) — and locates the bite at the **functional** end of the formal/functional cut ([`claim/formal-competence-aann-ceiling`](findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md) the tight-concord formal contrast). **Not a model ranking** (prediction 3 decorrelates magnitude from competence; no in-repo cross-task tabulation), **no human magnitude comparison** (only the dative *direction* is human-anchored), **"comparable general competence" flagged an unmeasured background premise**. `refines` [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md); `depends-on` [`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md) + [`conjecture/dative-alternation-information-structure`](findings/conjectures/dative-alternation-information-structure.md) + [`open-question/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. **2026-06-21 (session 63):** a measurement-level sibling was named — [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) adds the prior question this essay's per-model-magnitude comparison presupposes (*is the smaller magnitude bigger than its own run-to-run jitter?*); **no clause changed**, the "single run" honesty-box caveat given a named mechanism. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-21, session 64 — **trigger (a) FIRED**; originally draft session 63); **the project's SEVENTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the **measurement-level** sibling of the sixteenth ([`essay/concordant-verdict-hides-spread`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md)) and eleventh ([`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md)) — those two are about variation in the **phenomenon** (between-model split; between-model magnitude decorrelation); this one is one level down, about variation in the **measurement**. Written off the session-62 powered let-alone re-run ([`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md)), which ran a **byte-identical** instrument twice and found temperature-0 labels are **not** reproducible (claude 0.833→0.708 on the *identical* 24 items via 3 adverse flips; gpt 3/24 flips netting 0; **gemini deterministic**). Original contribution, a **reading discipline**: a single-run accuracy at temp 0 is a **draw**, not a fixed quantity, so it carries a **run-to-run jitter** that single-run Wilson/bootstrap CIs (which assume a fixed per-item Bernoulli rate) **structurally understate**; therefore **a between-X gap no larger than the jitter floor is not yet a finding** — rest weight on a small effect only if it clears the plausible jitter or the jitter is measured by repeated runs. Threads the needle with [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md): re-running the same hard instrument to "firm up" a null buys nothing, but re-running to **measure the noise floor** is licit (the trigger-(g) redirect). Bite is **uneven by design** — hardest at **small functional effects** ([`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md) end, where the ~±0.12 rivalled the effect), barely at all at **ceilings / clean separations** (the comp-correlative control PRESERVED 1.000; gemini deterministic), and **model-/instrument-specific** (not a transferable constant). **No new empirical claim, no human comparison.** Revision triggers: a repeated-run measurement on a non-near-chance instrument (would narrow the bite to hard/near-chance constructions); jitter shown to be a transferable constant (would harden into a numeric correction); an open-access source on temp-0 nondeterminism entering the repo (would ground the mechanism — queued in `wanted.md`, **not** in-repo, **not** fabricated); a small-but-real effect re-run and found stable (graduates it past this read). **Revision (session 64): trigger (a) FIRED** — [`result/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) ran the byte-identical instrument **K=5** and **narrowed** the essay: jitter is **ceiling-protected** (comp-corr range 0.000 vs let-alone up to 0.121) → "draws **on hard near-chance functional instruments**"; **model-specific** (gpt ~±0.12 / claude ~0.06 / gemini ~0.03; trigger (b) un-fired); "gemini deterministic" → "**most stable**" (2/33 churn); and gpt's residual **survives** the jitter (trigger (d) case: de-noised majority-vote 0.606, every one of 5 runs < 0.90). `refines` [`essay/concordant-verdict-hides-spread`](findings/essays/concordant-verdict-hides-spread.md); `depends-on` [`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md) + [`result/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) + [`essay/capability-split`](findings/essays/capability-split.md) + [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md) + [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`concept/formal-vs-functional-competence`](base/concepts/formal-vs-functional-competence.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-21, session 69); **the project's EIGHTEENTH essay** (methodological / philosophical track). Original contribution, a **design-epistemics rule** drawn from the function-word probe's session-68 overturn: **a control covariate that is *degenerate* — zero (or near-zero) within-condition variance, hence perfectly collinear with the manipulation — cannot be "controlled for" by regression or stratification; it must be designed out at construction time, not modelled out at analysis time.** Worked case: the function-word swap's orthographic length-delta is constant (+1) in the function arm, so stratifying collapses to the hard-matched set and regression identifies the contrast only off the +1 stratum — the length-neutral items a relaxation would add **never enter the bearing contrast** (the reason [`decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching`](decisions/resolved/function-word-count-vs-matching.md) overturned the relax-length default). Draws the **line** at within-condition variance (comfortable case: variance present → statistical control fine; **genuinely hard middle**: tiny-but-nonzero variance → burden shifts to construction; degenerate: design-out is the only valid control) and prices the **cost** (design-out constrains stimulus supply — the operationalization-vs-power tension, in the probe's own collapse numbers). `refines` [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) ("analysis cannot manufacture information the design did not put there") + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) (a parameter that must be *fixed* vs one that must be *varied* to be read); `depends-on` [`resource/subtlex-us-frequency`](base/resources/subtlex-us-frequency.md) + [`conjecture/function-word-substitutability`](findings/conjectures/function-word-substitutability.md). **No new empirical claim, no human comparison** (`internal-contrast-only` probe). (**methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-21, session 75); **the project's NINETEENTH essay** (lexical / philosophical track), written in the interval between the now-ratified lexical bridging-context design and its (unrun) probe. Original contribution, a conceptual distinction: a **graded sense scale** (cross-item: the model rank-orders usage pairs the way humans do — what [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) established) and **graded sense commitment** (within-item: lower confidence / declined binary on the single genuinely-ambiguous use — the unrun Prediction 4) are **logically independent**; v1 established only the former. Argues the first-class **null** — "graded scale, **ungraded** commitment," a smooth relatedness ordering with a confident discrete pick on every individual bridging use — is a **substantive behavioral finding** about machine sense (gradience in the aggregate ledger, none in the moment), contrasted against the lexicographer's *individual* indeterminacy on bridging uses. Frames the within-item distributional shadow as **three** live outcomes (commitment that survives the context control / ungraded commitment / commitment that evaporates under the control), and ties the fork to what distributional competence recovers ([`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md), [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md)). Three load-bearing disciplines: **behavior, not representation**; **usage-similarity, not certified sense co-presence** (the ratified anchor cap); the **contrast must clear** or there is nothing to read. Four revision triggers (positive-survives-control / the null / B–C disagreement-or-Route-3-collapse / a representational instrument); honesty box. **No new empirical claim, no human comparison beyond v1's usage-similarity-capped cross-item monotonicity.** `refines` + `depends-on` [`conjecture/lexical-sense-gradience`](findings/conjectures/lexical-sense-gradience.md); `depends-on` [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + [`open-question/lexical-bridging-context-gradience`](findings/open-questions/lexical-bridging-context-gradience.md) + [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md) + [`concept/referential-meaning`](base/concepts/referential-meaning.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md); `contingent-on: []`. (**lexical / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-23, session 92); **the project's TWENTIETH essay** (methodological / philosophical track), the generalization of the session-91 forced-both NULL. Original contribution: a behavioral probe's stimulus **premises** must be certified by a **certifier tripod** — independent of the model under test (anti-circularity), human bearing only via an *existing* resource (no human subjects), in place before the run — and when a *required* premise is readable **only** by a fresh human subject or the model-under-test, with no pre-encoding resource, it has **no admissible certifier** and the item is **uncertifiable from in-repo means**. Worked case: the forced-both in-item balance check ([`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md)). Placed as a **third** thing, distinct from [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) (conclusion-side) and [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md) (which assumes a construction-time fix); the **escape is the anchor discipline** (an existing human-labeled resource), the **honest price** of two good rules (no-human-subjects + anti-circularity). **Trigger (a) partially exercised the same session** by the SemEval co-activation scout ([`resource/semeval2017-pun-corpus`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md)): the escape lifts *co-activation* (via stimulus redesign), but the *in-item balance* premise still has no admissible certifier — confirmation, not refutation. `refines` [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md); `depends-on` [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md) + [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-23; **methodological / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md`](findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23, session 93; trigger (b) attempted-and-not-met logged session 94 — the forced-both v2 build tried the argued transfer-to-item and a fresh critic ruled it not arguable, fresh corroboration of the essay's core); **the project's TWENTY-FIRST essay** (lexical / methodological track), generalizing the session-93 ratification of [`decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns`](decisions/resolved/sense-coactivation-anchor-semeval-puns.md). Original contribution: a distinction between a **co-presence premise** (two senses are both in play in an item — existential, on/off) and a **balance premise** (neither of the two dominates — relative, graded), and the **asymmetry** that an *attested* ambiguity discharges the first and is **silent by type** on the second (a presence record is the wrong object to measure a salience weighting). Vivid case: a homographic pun *guarantees* co-presence (the joint requirement makes the joke) yet the genre's setup/punchline mechanics *bias against* balance, so the resource that best certifies co-presence is among the worst-placed to certify no-dominance. **Anchor rule** that follows: a resource may soundly anchor co-presence while *inventing* an anchor for balance, so the two must be sourced separately and the balance source must be graded and item-transferable (the word-grain [`resource/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms`](base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md) is the right *type* but still owes an argued transfer-to-item step). `refines` [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) (sharpens its escape: arriving-certified is **premise-relative**); serves [`essay/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability`](findings/essays/layer-specialness-vs-always-resolvability.md) (why Q1-ii's separate dominance step is type-correctness, not caution). `depends-on` the two resolved decisions + [`result/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1`](findings/results/forced-both-lexical-build-attempt-v1.md) + [`resource/semeval2017-pun-corpus`](base/resources/semeval2017-pun-corpus.md) + [`resource/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms`](base/resources/homonym-meaning-dominance-norms.md) + [`concept/polysemy`](base/concepts/polysemy.md). Four revision triggers; honesty box. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-23; **lexical / methodological track**)
- [`findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) — status: **revised** (2026-06-23 created session 95; revised through 2026-06-24 session 98 — trigger (d) fired s96, trigger (e) FULLY DISCHARGED s97 Borsboom + s98 Campbell & Fiske); **the project's TWENTY-SECOND essay** (methodological / philosophical track). Original contribution, a **reframing-plus-diagnosis**: the project's accumulated operationalization-gate discipline (freeze-before-run, `internal-contrast-only`, "no admissible certifier," "design-out-not-model-out," "presence-is-not-balance") **is** construct validation in [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md)'s sense, and the **no-human-subjects rule removes the criterion-oriented leg by rule** (predictive/concurrent validation needs "an independent criterion measure on the same subjects"; the project's subjects are models and fresh human subjects are barred), leaving **nomological-net construct validity as the only available form**. That single fact **predicts** the project's four recurring terminal states: `internal-contrast-only` = construct validity with the criterion leg amputated; "no admissible certifier" = a missing **observable node** in the net (Cronbach & Meehl's admissibility principle 3); the **two-edged negative** = disconfirmation falling on the whole net (their three-way charge — test / theory / design, "any link in the chain may be wrong" — the classical form of [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)'s typology); design-out / presence-is-not-balance = construct-instrument correspondence hygiene. Identifies [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md) as the project's **nomological-net-elaboration engine** (principle 4: "'Learning more about' a … construct is … elaborating the nomological network"). The honest price: without a criterion nothing outside the net pins the construct, so the freeze-and-rung discipline is load-bearing, and the criterion leg was **surrendered on purpose** for auditable anchoring. `refines` [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md) + [`essay/design-out-not-model-out`](findings/essays/design-out-not-model-out.md); `depends-on` [`source/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity`](base/sources/cronbach-meehl-1955-construct-validity.md) + [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md) + [`essay/presence-is-not-balance`](findings/essays/presence-is-not-balance.md) + [`essay/cross-level-convergence-ladder`](findings/essays/cross-level-convergence-ladder.md). **Revised 2026-06-24 (session 96 — trigger (d) FIRED):** two post-1955 validity sources ingested — [`source/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment`](base/sources/messick-1995-validity-of-psychological-assessment.md) (now the essay states its *design-out → construct-irrelevant-variance* and *presence-is-not-balance → construct-underrepresentation* mappings in Messick's **verbatim, sourced** vocabulary) and [`source/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks`](base/sources/freiesleben-2026-construct-validity-llm-benchmarks.md) (an independent measurement-philosophy preprint making the project's own framing choice — nomological net over causal/inferential — for LLM capability benchmarks). New section "Does the reconstruction match the post-1955 consensus?" answers: **largely yes** (Messick's unification, with the project as a limiting case; Freiesleben's LLM-domain corroboration), with one honest **gap** (the consequential/value aspect Messick adds, untheorized here) and one new **sharpening** — a *second amputation*: the project is barred from Borsboom's **causal/realist** validation leg too (it declines to assert the construct lives in the model), so the nomological net is the only one of the three classical routes its constraints leave available. **Revised 2026-06-24 (session 97 — trigger (e) Borsboom leg) + (session 98 — trigger (e) Campbell & Fiske leg):** both validity primaries are now in-repo, so trigger (e) is **fully discharged** — the causal/realist "second amputation" leg cites [`source/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity`](base/sources/borsboom-2004-concept-of-validity.md) directly (s97), and the convergent/discriminant + multitrait–multimethod vocabulary cites [`source/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm`](base/sources/campbell-fiske-1959-mtmm.md) directly (s98), each a secondary→primary upgrade with the secondary characterizations confirmed consistent (no correction). The essay now rests on five methodology primaries; **only trigger (f)** (the consequential/value aspect) stays dormant. `depends-on` the validity primaries added. **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (methodology sources, not human-comparison anchors).
