- [`findings/essays/two-distributional-hypotheses.md`](findings/essays/two-distributional-hypotheses.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-24, session 103); **the project's TWENTY-THIRD essay** (distributional / philosophical track). Original contribution, a **sorting**: "the distributional hypothesis" is **two distinct ideas**, not one — Harris's is **form-internal** (a within-language contrast measure, "difference of meaning correlates with difference of distribution," p. 156, primary-read), Firth's is **situated** (collocation as one mode of meaning among several, always in a "context of situation" — secondary-sourced via Brunila & LaViolette 2022, Firth primary not consulted). The next-token / embedding objective instantiates the **Harris** reading almost line-for-line and **not** the Firth one (the situational surround is precisely what a form-only model never sees — [`source/bender-koller-2020-climbing`](base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md)'s "a system trained only on form has a priori no way to learn meaning"). So NLP's Firth slogan ("you shall know a word by the company it keeps") **borrows Firth's words for Harris's idea**, narrowing Firth to the form-internal residue and **re-labelling, not resolving**, the grounding question: a correctly-sorted distributional success names its Harris ancestor precisely and leaves the Firth (situated) and Bender–Koller (world-relation) questions exactly where they were. Takes **no side** on the [`source/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference`](base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md) counter-position (inferential-role meaning without reference); its job is upstream — fixing *which* distributional hypothesis is on the table. Revision trigger: if a later session reaches the Firth primary and finds the form-internal/situated divergence overstated by the secondary, revise or retract. `depends-on` [`source/harris-1954-distributional-structure`](base/sources/harris-1954-distributional-structure.md) + [`source/firth-1957-synopsis`](base/sources/firth-1957-synopsis.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) + [`source/bender-koller-2020-climbing`](base/sources/bender-koller-2020-climbing.md) + [`source/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference`](base/sources/piantadosi-hill-2022-meaning-without-reference.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-24; **distributional / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/frame-semantics-third-company.md`](findings/essays/frame-semantics-third-company.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-25, session 104); **the project's TWENTY-FOURTH essay** (distributional / constructional / philosophical track), the explicit **third panel** of [`essay/two-distributional-hypotheses`](findings/essays/two-distributional-hypotheses.md). Original contribution, a **three-way sorting** of what a word's "company" can be: adds **Fillmore's evoked frame** — a structured background of *relational world-knowledge* the word evokes, "any system of concepts related in such a way that to understand any one of them you have to understand the whole structure in which it fits" (Fillmore frame definition, secondary-sourced via metaphorhacker.net, no locator) — as a **third reading** of "knowing a word by its company," distinct from both Harris's co-occurrence neighbourhood and Firth's situation. The sharper question it raises: a frame is a structure of **inferential** relations among concepts, so whether a model "has the frame" is **not** the co-occurrence question the next-token objective demonstrably instantiates but the question of whether form-distribution *alone* can encode that structured inferential background — a special case of the live Piantadosi–Hill-vs-Bender–Koller dispute, **declined here**. Payoff is precision not progress: a distributional success names the **Harris** company precisely and is **silent** on the Fillmore frame (and on Firth's situation); the frame's silence is an *open question the sorting names*, not a deficit or a competence. Fillmore premise **secondary-and-preview-sourced** (never primary-read), revision trigger armed against it; Firth half secondary, only Harris primary-read. `depends-on` [`source/fillmore-1982-frame-semantics`](base/sources/fillmore-1982-frame-semantics.md) + [`source/harris-1954-distributional-structure`](base/sources/harris-1954-distributional-structure.md) + [`source/firth-1957-synopsis`](base/sources/firth-1957-synopsis.md) + [`concept/frame-and-prototype-semantics`](base/concepts/frame-and-prototype-semantics.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) + [`essay/two-distributional-hypotheses`](findings/essays/two-distributional-hypotheses.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-25; **distributional / constructional / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/constructional-meaning-meets-frame.md`](findings/essays/constructional-meaning-meets-frame.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-25, session 105); **the project's TWENTY-FIFTH essay** (constructional / philosophical track), the **grammatical companion** to [`essay/frame-semantics-third-company`](findings/essays/frame-semantics-third-company.md). Original contribution, a **sorting / cousin move**: the **argument-structure construction** (Goldberg) is itself a **frame-evoker**, doing for the grammar what Fillmore's frame does for the lexicon — a *conventional form* evokes a *structured inferential background its parts do not fully predict*. Where Fillmore's evoking form is a **word**, Goldberg's is an **argument-structure pattern**; the two are **cousins by inheritance, not coincidence** (Construction Grammar builds the "meaning" half of its form–meaning pairings *on* frame semantics — an in-repo-recorded dependence). The constructional case **sharpens** the `inferential` point to its limit: in the coercion examples the verb is held constant and *stripped* of the entailment (*Frank sneezed the tissue off the table* ⇒ the sneezing caused the tissue to move, though *sneeze* denotes no motion), so the construction's content is exactly an inference the parts cannot license. Payoff is precision: the framing names *what* the project's caused-motion / *way*-construction probes test a model against — the **construction's** evoked scene, not the **verb's** lexical frame — while **declining** (exactly as the companion essay does) the open Piantadosi–Hill-vs-Bender–Koller question of whether form-distribution alone can *encode* such a structured inferential background. **Both** founding premises are **secondary-only**: Goldberg 1995 (definition via Boas 2021 "Goldberg 1995: 4"; caused-motion examples via Boas CCxG "Goldberg 1995: 152"; the weakest p. 1 thesis via the IIT-Kanpur excerpt) and Fillmore 1982 (frame definition via metaphorhacker.net, **no locator**); revision trigger armed. `depends-on` [`concept/constructional-meaning`](base/concepts/constructional-meaning.md) + [`concept/frame-and-prototype-semantics`](base/concepts/frame-and-prototype-semantics.md) + [`concept/coercion`](base/concepts/coercion.md) + [`source/goldberg-1995-constructions`](base/sources/goldberg-1995-constructions.md) + [`source/goldberg-2006-constructions-at-work`](base/sources/goldberg-2006-constructions-at-work.md) + [`source/fillmore-1982-frame-semantics`](base/sources/fillmore-1982-frame-semantics.md) + [`essay/frame-semantics-third-company`](findings/essays/frame-semantics-third-company.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-25; **enriched 2026-06-25 session 109** with the usage-based 2006 dimension + a `depends-on` to the now-sourced Goldberg-2006 + a cross-link to the new [`theory/statistical-preemption-and-constructional-productivity`](findings/theory/statistical-preemption-and-constructional-productivity.md); the cousins-by-inheritance sorting unchanged, an enrichment not a trigger discharge; **constructional / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/gradient-from-overlap.md`](findings/essays/gradient-from-overlap.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-26, session 118); a **distributional / referential / philosophical-track** essay, the first to bring the freshly-ingested prototype primaries to bear on the project's own lexical gradience result. Original contribution, a **sorting** of what a typicality/relatedness *gradient* ever licenses about a *representation*: Rosch & Mervis 1975 founded the prototype result by *deriving* graded typicality from attribute **overlap** ("networks of overlapping attributes … in proportion to the extent to which they bear a family resemblance," p. 575; Spearman 0.84–0.94, p < .001, p. 582) and **explicitly declined a learning/formation processing model** ("the present research was not intended to provide a processing model of the learning of categories or formation of prototypes," p. 574) — from which the essay *infers* (its reading, not their words) that no stored prototype is posited for the gradient to be evidence *for*. So the project's "**monotonicity, not representation**" caution ([`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md)) is **fidelity to the prototype tradition's own discipline, not a machine-specific deflation**: a gradient underdetermines a stored representation symmetrically, for people and models. Consequence: "**prototype-consistent**" and "**merely distributional**" are **not rival readings** of the model's gradient but the **same overlap-derived shape** — so the worry is **re-located, not dissolved**. The surviving open question is sharpened to *which overlap space* the model's gradient lives in — Rosch's **human-listed attributes** vs the model's **distributional context** — left open as the standing [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) question (v1's topic-control "substantially survives" but is flagged "model-internal," bounding not dissolving it). Backstops the discipline of [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) (gives the "behaviour, not representation" rule its rationale). Rosch & Mervis quotes **primary-direct**; the Rosch 1975b graded-typicality/priming lines **secondary-only** (via her 1978 retrospective), flagged in place. **None of Rosch & Mervis / Rosch 1975b / Wittgenstein is a human anchor** (theory-grounding only). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison beyond what v1 states.** `depends-on` [`source/rosch-mervis-1975-family-resemblances`](base/sources/rosch-mervis-1975-family-resemblances.md) + [`source/rosch-1975-cognitive-representations`](base/sources/rosch-1975-cognitive-representations.md) + [`source/wittgenstein-1953-philosophical-investigations`](base/sources/wittgenstein-1953-philosophical-investigations.md) + [`concept/frame-and-prototype-semantics`](base/concepts/frame-and-prototype-semantics.md) + [`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). (created 2026-06-26; **distributional / referential / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/two-tags-molecularist-bet.md`](findings/essays/two-tags-molecularist-bet.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-26, session 119); a **distributional / inferential / philosophical-track** essay that writes the case [`meaning-senses.md`](meaning-senses.md) invited ("Should `distributional` and `inferential` collapse… Probably no — but write the case explicitly when it next matters"). Original contribution, a **molecularist reading of the project's own typology**: keeping the two tags apart presupposes a *principled, bounded meaning-constitutive subset* distinct from the whole co-occurrence web — and that presupposition just **is** the **molecularist** disjunct of the holism axis ([`concept/semantic-holism`](base/concepts/semantic-holism.md)'s own hook: "if the inferential web and the distributional web are the same holistic object, the two tags track one thing; if molecularism is right, there is a principled subset that pulls them apart"). So the provisional "don't collapse" is a tacit **molecularist bet** — in Dummett's shape (content tied to "the theorems which relate to whole sentences," essay II p. 37, primary). Molecularism's bill is the **which-inferences-are-constitutive** problem, which re-invokes the analytic/synthetic line Quine attacked (synonymy "no less in need of clarification than analyticity itself," §I; "back at the problem of analyticity," §IV) — the molecularist charge being "an unstable resting point" (Dummett source S3, **secondary** via SEP). The essay's sharpest move: the project pays the bill **by stipulation, not solution** — the `inferential` indicator (inference-*preservation* on **frozen minimal pairs**, the construction-licensed entailment) **stipulates** the constitutive subset per probe by experimental design rather than deriving it, and even that stipulated subset is **instrument-fragile** (the conative NLI-vs-forced-choice split). Payoff is precision: the open issue is **re-located onto an unpaid bill**, not resolved. Structural-not-doctrinal caveat load-bearing (the *method* bets molecularism; no one signed up for the doctrine). `depends-on` [`source/dummett-1975-what-is-a-theory-of-meaning`](base/sources/dummett-1975-what-is-a-theory-of-meaning.md) + [`source/quine-1951-two-dogmas`](base/sources/quine-1951-two-dogmas.md) + [`concept/semantic-holism`](base/concepts/semantic-holism.md) + [`concept/inferential-meaning`](base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-26; **distributional / inferential / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/compositionality-asymptote-not-wall.md`](findings/essays/compositionality-asymptote-not-wall.md) — status: **draft** (2026-06-27, session 125); a **constructional / distributional / philosophical-track** essay built off the s124 Montague ingest ([`source/janssen-zimmermann-montague-semantics-sep`](base/sources/janssen-zimmermann-montague-semantics-sep.md)). Original contribution, an **asymptote-vs-wall structural diagnosis**: the project's behavioral method falls short of *two* philosophical targets in two *different shapes*. **Compositionality (Montague's homomorphism — "Syntax is an algebra, semantics is an algebra, and meaning is a homomorphism between them," §3.2) is an asymptote**: behavior reaches only the homomorphism's *extensional shadow* (the systematicity signature — the comparative-correlative negative×negative=positive item "a model reading only one clause would answer *decrease*. All three models answer *increase* (100%)"; coercion's verb-overriding inference), which **beats the simplest part-blind distributional null** but never *completes* the inference to "the model **realizes** the homomorphism," because finite behavior fixes a function's *graph* not its *form*, and the residue is "narrow[ed] … [but they] do not eliminate" plus the standing behavior-vs-mechanism gap ([`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md)). **Reference, by contrast, is a wall** ([`essay/reference-as-premise-bound`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md)): "premise-bound, not evidence-bound," no probe moves it at all. The difference is in *kind* (monotone-narrowing-without-completion vs no-narrowing) and is *consistent with* — though it does not prove (a missing-instrument confound is conceded) — why the compositionality program keeps buying evidence while the reference cell saturated after one round. Two citation consequences: cite a compositional positive **by the null it beats, never as realizing the homomorphism**; treat the homomorphism question as **productive-open**, not principled-closed. Montague target in-repo at **secondary** strength (SEP survey; PTQ primary still wanted); `referential` tag is the contrast pole only. `refines` [`concept/compositionality`](base/concepts/compositionality.md); `depends-on` that page + [`source/janssen-zimmermann-montague-semantics-sep`](base/sources/janssen-zimmermann-montague-semantics-sep.md) + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) + [`result/comparative-correlative-covariation-v2`](findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v2.md) + [`result/caused-motion-minimal-pair-divergence-v1`](findings/results/caused-motion-minimal-pair-divergence-v1.md) + [`result/way-construction-traversal-v1`](findings/results/way-construction-traversal-v1.md) + [`theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md) + [`essay/reference-as-premise-bound`](findings/essays/reference-as-premise-bound.md) + [`essay/two-distributional-hypotheses`](findings/essays/two-distributional-hypotheses.md) + [`essay/undischargeable-negative`](findings/essays/undischargeable-negative.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison.** (created 2026-06-27; **constructional / distributional / philosophical track**)
- [`findings/essays/predictive-objective-favors-accumulation.md`](findings/essays/predictive-objective-favors-accumulation.md) — status: **revised** (created s131; revised s138, and again reacting to the s141 within-verbal confirm — recorded s142: the antecedent moved from "weakly supported across a domain mismatch" to **supported on a clean within-verbal contrast** [M2 discharged, 3/3, leave-one-out robust]; still conditional, mechanism still labeled speculation, no human baseline); a **constructional / inferential / distributional / philosophical-track** essay. Original contribution, a **conditional** reading of the add-easy/cancel-hard asymmetry: *if* it survives the generalization test, it is the **behavioral fingerprint of a next-token predictive objective** — a construction's *added* inference (caused-motion's "the object moved" 90–100%, the way-construction's traversal 77.8–100%, 3/3 models) aligns **with** predicting the high-probability continuation (monotone, objective-aligned), whereas *cancelling* a lexical default (the conative's suppression — off-ceiling and model/instrument-dependent: NLI [58.3, 0.0, 66.7] pp, FC [66.7, 33.3, 83.3] pp at a transitive default of 91.7–100%, [`result/conative-cancel-direction-v2`](findings/results/conative-cancel-direction-v2.md)) works **against** a strong lexical prior (objective-hostile). So "license easier than suppress" is what meaning-as-prediction **predicts**. **Three honesty rails:** the generalization is the conjecture's **open** forward bet (`status: proposed`), so the essay is explicitly conditional and does NOT assert it as established; the mechanism is carried as the conjecture's **labeled speculation**, deflationary-compatible, never upgraded; both directions are **bounded** (the add direction's withholding is explicit-outcome parsing, not world-model integration — [`result/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b`](findings/results/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b.md) implicit-wk 90–100%), so the claim is only about *relative* reliability, never a deep competence the models have/lack. Revision triggers ride on the conjecture's own falsifiers (a matched ceiling-controlled battery showing **symmetric** add/cancel; or the asymmetry **reversing** for some construction class). **Sibling-distinct** from [`essay/gradient-from-overlap`](findings/essays/gradient-from-overlap.md) (representation underdetermination), [`essay/inference-default-coincidence`](findings/essays/inference-default-coincidence.md) (where add CAN'T be measured because the default does the work; this is why CANCEL is harder than ADD where both ARE measurable), and [`essay/compositionality-asymptote-not-wall`](findings/essays/compositionality-asymptote-not-wall.md). **No new empirical claim; no human comparison** (off-ceiling de-confounding arms are `internal-contrast-only`). `refines` + `depends-on` [`conjecture/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry`](findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md); `depends-on` the two result pages + [`concept/distributional-meaning`](base/concepts/distributional-meaning.md) + [`concept/inferential-meaning`](base/concepts/inferential-meaning.md) + [`concept/coercion`](base/concepts/coercion.md) + [`theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md). (created 2026-06-28; **philosophical track**)

### Findings — claims / results / theory / open-questions

- [`findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md`](findings/claims/formal-competence-aann-ceiling.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-28); AANN acceptability ceiling is evidence of formal, not functional, linguistic competence. Grounded by Mahowald 2024 formal/functional distinction; anchored to [`resource/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli`](base/resources/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli.md).
- [`findings/claims/constructional-divergent-form-generalization-gap.md`](findings/claims/constructional-divergent-form-generalization-gap.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); LLMs track constructional form–meaning pairings "up to a point" but show a >40% generalization gap (GPT-o1) on syntactically-identical / semantically-divergent forms vs. a native-speaker baseline (≈0.90/≈0.83). The project's first claim with in-repo human-comparison empirical bearing. Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); sits at the theory ladder's Tier 3→4 boundary. `contingent-on: []`.
- [`findings/claims/cxg-probing-surprisal-validity.md`](findings/claims/cxg-probing-surprisal-validity.md) — status: proposed (2026-05-29); surprisal contrast on form–meaning minimal pairs is a valid (but bounded) operationalization of constructional-meaning *sensitivity*. Methodological counterpart to the AANN-ceiling claim. Anchored to `resource/mahowald-2023-aann-stimuli` (AANN-scoped); cross-construction generality stays provisional (`cxg-probing-anchor` resolved 2026-05-29, Option A).
- [`findings/claims/preference-commitment-dissociation-aann-specific.md`](findings/claims/preference-commitment-dissociation-aann-specific.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-15); **the honest close of the generality question** — on the evidence so far, the forced-choice-paraphrase-vs-entailment ("preference without commitment") dissociation is **AANN-specific**. It replicates across two disjoint AANN item sets ([`result/aann-inferential-v4`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v4.md) paraphrase Δ² +0.78/+0.70/+0.96; [`result/aann-inferential-v6`](findings/results/aann-inferential-v6.md) +0.875/+0.575/+0.90) but **does not reproduce on the conative** across two independent verb samples ([`result/conative-preference-commitment-v1`](findings/results/conative-preference-commitment-v1.md) INCONCLUSIVE, Δ²_pref non-positive in all three; [`result/conative-commitment-replication-v2`](findings/results/conative-commitment-replication-v2.md) the lone counter-signal collapsing +0.46→+0.04), **in either direction** — the apparent conative exception was verb-set-specific noise. Draws three calibrated consequences: the dissociation does not generalize beyond AANN on current evidence; a forced-choice "preference" can be driven by a bare lexical cue (so a preference shift is not by itself evidence of constructional inference); the result is construction-particular. Calibrated hard to "AANN-specific *so far*" (only **one** alternative construction tested; a third needs engineered headroom). `anchor: internal-contrast-only` (a within-model cross-construction contrast, inherited from its constituent results; no new human-comparison claim); `contingent-on: []`. Refines [`conjecture/preference-commitment-generality`](findings/conjectures/preference-commitment-generality.md) (tested → not confirmed), [`essay/preference-without-commitment`](findings/essays/preference-without-commitment.md), and the theory ladder. (**grammatical track**)
- [`findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-16, twentieth session); **LLM referential conventions are order-sensitive (non-commutative) when the history carries disambiguating recency information.** Promoted from the clean ceiling positive in [`result/relational-spontaneous-recency-a`](findings/results/relational-spontaneous-recency-a.md): when a coined term is reassigned across stamped rounds so the content-set is symmetric and only recency disambiguates, both models (claude, gemini) recover it by its **most-recent binding** spontaneously (latest-binding 1.000, position at chance, DIRECT on-demand 1.000). **Contradicts** [`conjecture/commutative-convention`](findings/conjectures/commutative-convention.md) (retired); **refines** [`concept/relational-meaning`](base/concepts/relational-meaning.md) (places the models on the order-sensitive side, but at its *bottom rung* — a thin latest-binding-wins rule, not constitution). Scope: internal-contrast-only (no human comparison); one operationalization; thin≠rich; "spontaneous" = query-not-directed, not cue-free. **Strengthened 2026-06-17** by the implicit-reassignment control ([`result/relational-implicit-reassignment-control`](findings/results/relational-implicit-reassignment-control.md)): with the explicit "was reassigned" flag removed, the behaviour persists at ceiling — not a wording artifact (revision trigger 2 bounded, scope limit 4 tightened to *flag-not-directed*). `anchor: internal-contrast-only`; `contingent-on: []`. (**relational axis**)
- [`findings/claims/dative-pronominality-partial-reach.md`](findings/claims/dative-pronominality-partial-reach.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-20, session 56); **recipient pronominality — the LARGEST information-structure factor in the human dative (−1.48) — is a documented partial-reach (Option C), not a behavioral finding.** Realizes Option C of [`decisions/resolved/dative-pronominality-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/dative-pronominality-operationalization.md): under pure autonomy (no prompt logprobs) **no controlled forced-choice minimal pair isolates pronominality from length and givenness by construction** — a pronoun is a property of the scored sentence (so the within-item length-immunity collapses to a between-item contrast), is intrinsically the shorter constituent (so it reintroduces the short-before-long confound and cannot fill the given-but-longer dissociation cell), and is near-collinear with givenness. The provisional Option-A default (length-matched pronoun-vs-name) was *rejected* — its repeated-name-penalty confound runs in the *predicted* direction and prosodic weight is not dissociable by construction. So pronominality is reported **only on the human side** (where the corpus fit weights it most heavily of the information-structure factors) and left as the documented edge of the instrument's reach — a "text alone cannot reach this" closure analogous to the relational transcript-ceiling and third-construction headroom closures. **No probe, $0; makes no "model can/can't" claim.** Human-anchored to [`resource/languageR-dative-corpus`](base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md); bounds [`result/dative-information-structure-v1`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md)/[`v2`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v2.md) (the *reached* givenness result, untouched). `anchor: human-anchored`; `contingent-on: []`. (**grammatical track**)
- [`findings/claims/lexical-graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md`](findings/claims/lexical-graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) — status: **supported** (2026-06-22, session 77); **on human-rated usage-similarity-midpoint (bridging) pairs, all three panel models place the pair at an intermediate relatedness position but meet it with clear-item confidence and almost never decline — a graded SCALE with ungraded COMMITMENT** (behavioral; usage-similarity-capped). The empirical statement [`essay/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment`](findings/essays/graded-scale-ungraded-commitment.md) anticipated, now carried by [`result/lexical-bridging-context-v1`](findings/results/lexical-bridging-context-v1.md) (3/3 models; clear-class precondition met; commitment null corroborated across confidence (B), decline (C), and dispersion (A)). Scope/caps: usage-similarity not sense co-presence; behavioral not representational; small lemma-clustered N (24 bridging/17 lemmas); the commitment null is the shadow-robust part, the position/scale reading partly tracks topic (Q3 r 0.32–0.53). Anchored to [`resource/dwug-usage-graphs`](base/resources/dwug-usage-graphs.md) (clear poles supplemented by [`resource/wic-word-in-context`](base/resources/wic-word-in-context.md)); `contingent-on: []`. (**lexical track**)
- [`findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md) — status: draft (updated 2026-05-31); the project's first theory page. A five-tier evidence ladder (form-acceptability < surprisal-contrast < gradient semantic tracking < generalization < inference-licensing) placing each claim/conjecture/result; brackets the grounding axis; flags the relational axis as future work. Holds the eleven own-design constructional results; the 2026-05-31 consolidation discharged the "first lexical probe" revision trigger and brought its lexical/grounding cross-references current (pointing to the continuum page for depth).
- [`findings/theory/lexicon-grammar-continuum.md`](findings/theory/lexicon-grammar-continuum.md) — status: draft (updated 2026-05-31); the project's **second theory page — the lexical↔grammatical connection** (Tom's steer). Argues the lexical and grammatical wedges are the two ends of one CxG form–meaning cline (a word = a maximally specific construction) probed by **one test**: does a meaning gradient beat the distributional shadow (context similarity for words; n-gram/form for constructions)? The project now has a positive that beats the shadow on **both** ends ([`result/lexical-sense-gradience-v1`](findings/results/lexical-sense-gradience-v1.md) + the CC results). The 2026-05-31 consolidation absorbed the full lexical/bridge/grounding state: clause (b) discreteness is a **powered null** (v3), the coercion bridge **partially de-confounds** (v1→v2, fragile fine-scale residual), and the grounding axis stands at **two bounded negatives** (perceptual-moderation + image redundancy). Governs the bridge probe [`design/coercion-as-sense-modulation-v1`](../experiments/designs/coercion-as-sense-modulation-v1.md) (coercion = grammar-induced lexical sense shift).
- [`findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md`](findings/theory/situating-llm-meaning.md) — status: draft (created 2026-05-31; **relational cell synced 2026-06-16; enriched 2026-06-19** with the order-sensitive composition rung); the project's **third theory page — the philosophical-map synthesis**. Positions the four axes' findings (constructional ladder, lexical gradience positive, grounding nulls, relational result, cross-axis dissociation) against the classical positions now in the concept layer, stating for each which the evidence **supports / strains / is silent on**. Verdict (a calibrated sketch, not a settled location): LLM meaning, where the project can see it, lives **model-internal** as a graded, compositional, *thin*-inferential **use**-structure that **beats but does not escape** the distributional shadow — while the three between/beyond loci (referential/world, perceptual grounding, between-agents) are each **silent or bounded-negative**; a deflation-leaning but **not** eliminativist picture (the descriptivist middle the charter chose). **2026-06-16:** the relational cell is updated for the Option-A falsification — still **negative on constitution** (the order-sensitivity is thin), but the clean commutative-aggregation reading is now falsified where order disambiguates ([`claim/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment`](findings/claims/relational-order-sensitive-reassignment.md)); the "commutativity stays under perturbation" prediction **resolved against**. `contingent-on: []`.
- [`findings/theory/statistical-preemption-and-constructional-productivity.md`](findings/theory/statistical-preemption-and-constructional-productivity.md) — status: **draft** (created 2026-06-25, session 109); the project's **fourth theory page** — a synthesis pairing Goldberg-2006's two usage-based **learning levers** onto the existing constructional apparatus. **Productivity** (degree of openness / type frequency) ↔ the **held-out-item generalization test** already built into the Tier-3 rung and the *way*/caused-motion conjectures' confirm bars; **statistical preemption** (meaning-conditioned indirect negative evidence) ↔ a **blocking/dispreference** signature for which the project so far has only *preconditions* (the coercion line's cancellability + form-keying — [`result/argument-structure-coercion-v2`](findings/results/argument-structure-coercion-v2.md), [`result/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c`](findings/results/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c.md), [`result/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b`](findings/results/coercion-implicit-cue-v2b.md)), **not** an isolated preemption test. That asymmetry — solid productivity hooks, only preconditions for preemption — is the synthesis's finding. **Sharp bound (load-bearing):** Goldberg 2006 is a theory of **human** acquisition and **NOT a human anchor** (no `anchors:` link, by design); a model matching a productivity/preemption *prediction* is **not** evidence it learned as humans do — distributional structure can mimic both productivity-like generalization and frequency-driven "blocking" without the meaning-conditioned mechanism, the unsolved [`open-question/constructional-vs-frequency-confound`](findings/open-questions/constructional-vs-frequency-confound.md) restated. **No new empirical claim;** names a *framing* (not a design) for a future preemption-vs-productivity probe; grounding question left open. `refines` [`theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms`](findings/theory/constructional-meaning-in-llms.md); `depends-on` [`source/goldberg-2006-constructions-at-work`](base/sources/goldberg-2006-constructions-at-work.md) + the four results/two conjectures/two open-questions it cites. `contingent-on: []`. (**constructional / philosophical track**)

### Findings — results

- [`findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1.md`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-28, session 127); **the natural-language-baseline MAGNITUDE run — BUILT + FROZEN, then DEFERRED at the adequacy-audit gate (pre-run-critic NO-GO).** Authored the fluent referent-naming channel v2's Limitation 1 owed (1158 NL descriptions, claude, names allowed; competent on inspection), ran the TEXT-NL arm (**not saturated**: acc .833/.767/.842; `sep_nl_i` strata under-det 18 / sat 77, both clearing the ≥15 floor) and the held-out adequacy audit (gpt+gemini, held out from the claude author). **Audit OUT OF BAND** (two-auditor mean high-recovery **0.342** < the `[0.60,0.95]` floor) → a fresh independent pre-run-critic **NO-GO that defers the magnitude read; the reused IMAGE arm was NOT read.** The critic verified by hand the NO-GO is a **scorer-validity artifact, not a degenerate channel** (~64/70 "none" items are faithful category recoveries the *literal-target-word-lemma* scorer mis-scored — thymus→thyme, ara→macaw, mescal→mezcal, supporter→jockstrap, nan→Nan River; the v2 design-B.4 gap). **Prediction 3 ("narrow headroom") stays UNTESTED** (neither supported nor refuted); the conjecture stays `proposed`. Makes **no** human-comparison claim (`anchor: internal-contrast-only`). Surfaces [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity.md) (a valid category-match re-grade; all frozen artifacts reusable, no re-authoring spend). **$3.115 billed** (descriptors $2.699 + TEXT-NL $0.363 + audit $0.039 + preflight $0.014). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v1.md`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-24, session 100); **the project's FIRST image-native selection RUN and first VWSD probe** — operationalizes the **gating shape** of [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) prediction 1 on a frozen 50-item SemEval-2023 VWSD EN-gold subset (3 arms: caption-based text-only selection [frozen separability covariate] / real-image selection / word-ablated distraction control), under the resolved DV decision [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv.md) (Option A, interaction-as-test-of-record, 5 mods). **Verdict: NEITHER CONFIRMS NOR FALSIFIES** the gating prediction. The **caption-text baseline SATURATED** (per-model .86–.88; 40/50 text-separable; under-determined bin 7 < the mod-1 floor 8 → **binned interaction suppressed** per the frozen fallback), the **distraction null is clean** (word-ablated gold-selection pooled .093 ≈ chance → selection is sense-driven, not salience), and **real images gave no broad lift** over their captions (gpt WORSE with images .60 vs .86; rescue only 4/16 text-failed cells) → a bounded reappearance of the redundancy null in an image-native selection task, **caption-leakage-confounded + underpowered**. Data fetched + checksummed (images out of git — redistribution unconfirmed). 450 finding-bearing calls, **$3.204 billed (3 arms) + $0.887 captions**; independent **pre-run critic GO** [barred any gating confirm/falsify claim; required binned interaction suppressed] + independent **post-run verifier REPRODUCED** every number. Human-anchored to [`resource/vwsd-semeval-2023`](base/resources/vwsd-semeval-2023.md). The conjecture stays `proposed`; prediction-1-as-written remains open for a future graded-image resource. (**multimodal axis**)
- [`findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-27, sessions 107/112/121); **the re-operationalized VWSD run — the first confirming-direction evidence on the project's grounding axis.** Fixes v1's three Limitations (non-caption **Option-B visual-form descriptor** baseline; stratified **N=120** clearing a **≥15/stratum** floor; raised claude image-arm `max_tokens`), completed across a multi-day split (day-1 text freeze s107, IMAGE arm s112, **DISTRACT control s121**). **Verdict: SUPPORTS the gating SHAPE of [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) prediction 1, 3/3 models in direction.** The word-ablated **DISTRACT null is CLEAN** (pooled .097 Wilson[.071,.132], no model LB > chance .10 → image lift is sense-driven, not salience), and the real image **rescues the descriptor-text-failed (under-determined) cells** (pooled .453 [.353,.558]; per-model claude .500 / gpt .303 / gemini .609, all > chance) while adding **no lift where the descriptor already separates** (saturated stratum Δ −.122). Caveats foregrounded: **gemini's Option-A floor is elevated** (.158, Wilson LB .104 > chance); **gpt degrades overall** (.725→.592, its gating support sign-only); the headroom **magnitude is inflated by the deliberately de-referented Option-B channel**, so this supports the **shape**, NOT the conjecture's "narrow headroom" magnitude bet (prediction 3); and it remains **gating-shape-on-binary-selection**, NOT prediction-1-as-written (no graded relatedness), NOT reference. 360 DISTRACT calls, **$3.763 billed** (two sub-batches under the $2.50 flag) + $0.062 preflight = $3.825 day total; images out of git (sha `b9f2f1e1…` re-verified). Independent **post-run verifier REPRODUCED** every number from raw (1440/1440 records consistent; all 3 binding conditions confirmed). Human-anchored to [`resource/vwsd-semeval-2023`](base/resources/vwsd-semeval-2023.md). The conjecture stays `proposed` (a later session may weigh `proposed → tested` + design the natural-language-baseline magnitude test). (**multimodal axis**)
- [`findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md`](findings/results/dative-information-structure-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20, session 51); **the dative alternation tracks information structure — a human-anchored Tier-2 panel CONFIRM (3/3).** Runs the frozen+certified instrument ([`stimuli.json` sha `0ffe3700…ababf`]) under the ratified operationalization [`decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator`](decisions/resolved/dative-anchor-and-indicator.md). All three panel models shift double-object-vs-prepositional-dative preference in the **human direction** (given recipient → DOC, given theme → PD) across a manipulation that holds length+animacy **identical by construction** (within-item shift provably immune to every length/position/order shortcut — build-certified, all 8 shortcut readers → shift 0), and the effect **survives the end-weight dissociation control** (given = the *longer* constituent) for all three. **Effect size sharply decorrelated** (gemini +0.524 ≫ claude +0.327 ≫ gpt +0.056, all bootstrap-LB > 0 → prediction 3 confirmed; gpt a weak-but-clearing CONFIRM). Secondary corpus-gradient Spearman ρ 0.48–0.83 (non-decisive, strengthens). 0 NA/retry/trunc; independent post-run verifier REPRODUCED from raw. Human-anchored to [`resource/languageR-dative-corpus`](base/resources/languageR-dative-corpus.md) (Bresnan et al. 2007 production surface). $1.578 billed (a disclosed $1.50 hard-stop-and-resume on gpt — budget gate, blind to analysis; total under the $5/day cap). The project's **first human-anchored Tier-2 positive of its own design**; the grammatical core returns. (created 2026-06-20)

- [`findings/results/function-word-modal-widening.md`](findings/results/function-word-modal-widening.md) — status: supported (2026-06-21, session 71); **the `will`→`would` modal NLI null does NOT generalize — it is a future→conditional fact, not a modal fact.** Widens the modal arm of [`result/function-word-swap-run-v2`](findings/results/function-word-swap-run-v2.md) to fire essay revision trigger (a). Per-arm flip_fn: **`will`→`would` replicates the null** (claude 0/20, gpt 0/20, gemini 3/20); **`must`→`might` (necessity→possibility) flips at CEILING in all three** (20/20 each); **`shall`→`should` (deontic obligation→advisory) SPLITS the panel** (gemini 0.778 reads *should* ≠ *required*; claude/gpt 0.056 collapse *should* ≈ *required*) — base-label agreement HIGH for every modal arm (1.0/1.0/0.89 for shall), so the nulls and split are interpretable, not measurement failures; controls because/some flip ~0.93–1.0, content control near-floor. The instrument registers a modal swap in proportion to how truth-conditionally "loud" it is: loud category-mismatch (must→might, all) > within-deontic-strength (shall→should, one model) > subtle future→conditional irrealis (will→would, none). **Caveat:** must→might crosses deontic→epistemic flavor (a category mismatch, the easy non-entailment) so it does NOT isolate a pure necessity-vs-possibility reading; shall→should is the clean within-scale test. Narrows the essay's blanket "modals are NLI-invisible" reading; vindicates its deeper "the instrument's calibration co-determines the result." Coherence echo: claude (and here gemini) read *some*→all as contradiction (scalar upper-bounding, cf. The richer finding is **why**: the marginal verb pool is **bimodal**, not a contestable band — low-propulsion physical verbs ("blinked the feather off the table") affirm the construction **at ceiling** (pooled 0.93, verb-independent coercion, like the *way*-construction), while cognition verbs ("knew the feather off the table") are off-ceiling only by being **anomalous** (pooled 0.17, all models reject), and anomalous verbs cannot carry the lexical-cue control frame — so a *usable* off-ceiling band does not exist. The conjecture's **second** failed generalization attempt (conative cancel-direction INCONCLUSIVE; caused-motion add-direction Option-C); neither falsifies it, but the generality bet is now un-instanced in **both** inference directions. - [`findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20); **the full Scivetti CxNLI base answer-key task** — panel NLI labels vs per-item gold on the **complete** 390-item Exp-1 set (all 8 constructions, 130/130/130), vs the ≈0.90 native-speaker baseline. **2/3 models match human** (claude 0.903 / gemini 0.915, CIs cover 0.90; gpt-5.4-mini 0.813 BELOW); the one cross-model failure is the phrasal scalar **let-alone** (0.46–0.67, near 3-way chance), not any argument-structure construction. **Discharges** [`result/cxnli-distinction-divergence-v1`](findings/results/cxnli-distinction-divergence-v1.md) limit 1 (full base set, not a 20-item subsample). Answer-key under possible contamination (the *failure* is the robust signal). - [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20); **the let-alone failure is largely an OUTPUT-CHANNEL artifact** — the witness-seeking control [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) prescribes. Re-ran the SAME 24 let-alone + 30 comparative-correlative (ceiling control) items under a **working surface** (step-by-step + `FINAL:` tag), format-only, gemini reasoning-effort held constant. **2/3 LIFT to the human ≈0.90 baseline on the same items** (claude 0.542→0.792, gemini 0.667→0.917; within-item sign test 7/1, p=0.035; control PRESERVED) → the session-57 scalar-phrasal dissociation was substantially a forced-single-token channel effect masking *scalar/serial* inference, **not** a content-type competence boundary. gpt-5.4-mini did **not** recover (0.375) but largely **declined** the surface (16/24 bare, 0 reasoning tokens) → channel **non-uptake**, not channel-controlled. Fires `output-channel-confound` trigger (a) + refines its scope (the cut is "is the inference serial," not "is it NLI"); trigger (b) stays open (needs uptake-inducing arm). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.3164. (0 NA / 162 calls; independent pre-run critic GO + post-run verifier REPRODUCED.)
- [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20); **forcing the weakest model to actually USE the working surface partly closes its let-alone gap but does not reach the human baseline** — the uptake-inducing arm session 58 named. Re-ran the SAME 24 let-alone + 30 comparative-correlative items with a **forced** 3-step decomposition (mandatory, construction-neutral, answer-blind; no demo items), single-variable vs session 58's *offered* surface. **Uptake INDUCED for all 3** (gpt's median let-alone completion 8→120 tokens, 24/24 worked, closing session 58's "channel-not-taken-up" gap). With the channel genuinely exercised, gpt rose 0.375→**0.583** (+0.21, 7/2, **but sign-test p=0.090 → UNCHANGED**, underpowered) and **stays BELOW** the ≈0.90 baseline where claude (0.833) / gemini (0.875) sit → a **partial** output-channel effect (part channel-bounded, part survives the exercised channel), the closest in-repo **trigger-(b) candidate**, not a clean firing. claude/gemini stay at baseline + control PRESERVED (scaffold benign). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-working-surface-v1.md); supports [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md). (0 NA / 162 calls; independent pre-run critic GO + post-run verifier REPRODUCED.)
- [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-20, session 62); **the POWERED re-run CONFIRMS gpt's below-baseline let-alone residual at higher N — but exposes ~12% temp-0 label stochasticity as the new binding limit, not item count.** The trigger-(g) powered re-run of session 60's partial witness: forced-decomposition instrument **byte-identical**, let-alone target enlarged **24→33** with the **9 DISJOINT** train-split items (0 shared premise/hyp pairs; 1-example train ⊆ these 9, so 33 = the human-anchored ceiling); comp-corr 30 control byte-identical. **gpt CONFIRMS-RESIDUAL** (combined **0.636** [0.466, 0.778], CI hi < 0.90 holds; test reproduced 0.583→0.583 *exactly* via offsetting flips, train 7/9=0.778), uptake induced 33/33, control PRESERVED → the cleanest in-repo [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) **trigger-(b)** channel-controlled residual (candidate→**fired**, magnitude-caveated). **New limit:** claude — a baseline-matcher — fell 0.833→**0.708** on the *identical* 24 items (3 adverse temp-0 flips; gpt churns too; gemini deterministic, at baseline 0.909), a per-run swing comparable to the residual gap → precision now bounded by **measurement noise**, redirect to repeated-runs (`essay/witness-seeking-economics` **trigger (g)** RESOLVED, the partial-witness slot's first resolved instance). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-forced-decomposition-v1.md); supports [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md) + [`essay/witness-seeking-economics`](findings/essays/witness-seeking-economics.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $0.3921. (0 NA / 189 calls; independent pre-run critic GO + post-run verifier REPRODUCED.) **→ Magnitude/determinism detail superseded by the K=5 measurement below (finding unchanged).**
- [`findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-repeated-runs-v1.md) — status: proposed (2026-06-21, session 64); **five repeated temp-0 runs PIN the let-alone jitter — it is ceiling-protected and model-specific, and gpt's below-baseline residual is robust to it.** The trigger-(g) / [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) trigger-(a) repeated-run measurement: the **byte-identical** forced-decomposition instrument scored **K=5** times at temp 0 over the **same frozen 63 items** (all shas == s62). **Trigger (a) FIRES (all three models):** the comp-corr ceiling control **did not jitter** (range 0.000 claude/gemini; 0.033 gpt) while near-chance let-alone swung (**gpt range 0.121**, claude 0.061, gemini 0.030) → jitter is **near-chance-concentrated, ceiling-protected, model-specific** (the ~±0.12 is *gpt's* number; trigger (b) un-fired). **gpt residual robust:** every one of 5 runs **< 0.90** (band [0.545, 0.667]); de-noised majority-vote **0.606** [0.437, 0.753] → session 62's CONFIRMS-RESIDUAL was **not** a low draw (trigger (d) case). **Refines s62:** "gemini deterministic" → "**most stable**" (2/33 churn); claude's s62 0.708 was a low draw (within-session test band [0.750, 0.792]); same-session spread a **lower bound** (claude's cross-session s60→s62 swing 0.125 > within-session test range 0.042). **Refines** [`result/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-let-alone-powered-rerun-v1.md); supports [`essay/point-estimate-is-a-draw`](findings/essays/point-estimate-is-a-draw.md) + [`essay/output-channel-confound`](findings/essays/output-channel-confound.md). Anchored to [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md); `contingent-on: []`. Cost $1.9642 (0 missing / 945 calls; independent pre-run critic GO + post-run verifier REPRODUCED).

### Experiments — designs

(Not part of the wiki tree, but indexed here for navigability.)

- [`experiments/designs/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline.md`](../experiments/designs/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline.md) — **BUILT + FROZEN session 127, then DEFERRED at the adequacy-audit gate (pre-run-critic NO-GO); the VWSD grounding-headroom NL-baseline MAGNITUDE follow-up. $3.115.** The fluent channel was authored (1158 NL descriptions, claude, names allowed; competent on inspection), the TEXT-NL arm ran (not saturated: acc .833/.767/.842; `sep_nl_i` under-det 18 / sat 77, both clearing the ≥15 floor), and the held-out adequacy audit ran — but it landed **OUT OF BAND** (two-auditor mean high-recovery **0.342** < the `[0.60,0.95]` floor) for a reason an independent critic verified is a **scorer-validity artifact, not a degenerate channel** (~64/70 "none" items are faithful category recoveries the literal-target-word-lemma scorer mis-scored). **Magnitude read deferred, IMAGE arm NOT read, prediction 3 UNTESTED** → [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-audit-v1.md); now gated on [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-recovery-scorer-validity.md) (a valid category-match re-grade; frozen artifacts reusable, no re-authoring spend). Answers [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md)'s first-class **Limitation 1** (the headroom magnitude is inflated by the deliberately de-referented Option-B channel, so v2 tested the gating *shape*, not prediction 3's "narrow headroom" *size*). The v1→v2→NL **symmetry**: v1 referent-NAMING captions **saturated**; v2 referent-BARRED descriptors **manufactured** headroom; the NL-baseline is the powered, stratified **fluent middle** — a competent natural-language candidate description (names allowed) on the SAME frozen 120, reusing the frozen **IMAGE** and the clean **DISTRACT** arms unchanged (only the new text channel is spent → cheap). Test of record = the **residual width** under a fluent channel (narrow → supports prediction 3; wide → refutes the size sub-bet, gating shape intact; both pre-registered first-class). Its load-bearing choice — what standard of "competence" the description meets — was **surfaced**, not smuggled, and **ratified cross-session session 123 (ADOPT-DEFAULT Q1-C)**: [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-nlbaseline-competence-dv.md) (fresh fluent descriptions + a held-out two-sided adequacy-audit band barring both an oracle and a degenerate channel; band edges + audit model + recovery-scoring rule deferred to the authoring session). The standard is now fixed in shape, so the design is **cleared to be frozen**; the result stays NOT cleared until a later session freezes the NL channel + audit + `sep_nl_i` (checksummed before the reused IMAGE arm is read), obtains a fresh pre-run-critic GO, and records a cap-clearing pre-flight. Narrow Q3 posture (selection accuracy, NOT prediction-1-as-written, NOT reference; all four VWSD caveats). `anchor: resource/vwsd-semeval-2023`. (**multimodal axis**)
- [`experiments/designs/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md`](../experiments/designs/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v2.md) — **FROZEN design (2026-06-25, session 106); the VWSD grounding-headroom re-operationalization — yardstick only, NO probe run, $0.** Implements the ratified gate [`decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv-v2`](decisions/resolved/vwsd-grounding-headroom-dv-v2.md) (ADOPT-DEFAULT) after the three first-class Limitations of [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-v1.md) (caption-leakage contamination of the separability covariate; floor-not-met/underpowered; claude reasoning-then-truncation). Freezes: **Q1 Option-B** sense-neutral visual-form **descriptor** baseline (generator prompt barred from naming the referent) + **Option-A** chance-floor calibration arm + **Option-C** per-item leak-audit covariate, all frozen+checksummed pre-image; **N = 120** stratified EN-gold draw (from a ~200 pool) clearing a re-stated **≥15 per-stratum floor**; per-model covariate frozen pre-image; **distraction null reported first**; **claude image-arm `max_tokens` 16→512** (condition d). The **result is NOT cleared** — gated on descriptors+leak-audit actually generated/frozen, EN images fetched+checksummed out of git, a **fresh pre-run-critic GO**, and a cap-clearing pre-flight (≈5 UTC-day split: descriptor/freeze day ≈$4.0, IMAGE 2 days, DISTRACT 2 days). Narrow Q3 posture (selection accuracy vs human gold, NOT prediction-1-as-written, NOT reference; all four VWSD caveats). `anchor: resource/vwsd-semeval-2023` (gold-test selection accuracy, gating-shape-only). (**multimodal axis**)

- [`experiments/designs/multimodal-grounding-image-v1.md`](../experiments/designs/multimodal-grounding-image-v1.md) — **draft (2026-05-31); the project's FIRST image-input probe** (conjecture predictions 2–3). Does showing a disambiguating image move the panel's graded sense-relatedness behavior **toward** the human signal, **keyed to where senses are visually distinct**? Anchor = WiC binary same/different labels (claims binary-scoped); images = a designed manipulation, sourced PD/CC0 from Wikimedia Commons (path verified live), downscaled + sha256-frozen before any model call. Conditions: text-only vs image+text, same panel/instrument. Governed by [`decisions/resolved/multimodal-panel-and-grounding-theory`](decisions/resolved/multimodal-panel-and-grounding-theory.md) (Q3=B GO) + [`decisions/resolved/multimodal-image-anchor`](decisions/resolved/multimodal-image-anchor.md) (Option A ratified). **RAN 2026-05-31 → redundancy null ([`result/multimodal-grounding-image-v1`](findings/results/multimodal-grounding-image-v1.md)).**

Tests whether genuine-homonym different-sense pairs form a separable low mode and whether the model separates same/different better for homonyms than polysemes. Reuses the resolved operationalization gate (no new decision). `anchor: resource/wic-word-in-context`; ~600 items, est. ≈$4.2 billed (pre-flight + drop-to-one-framing guard). **Carries real spend (unlike the $0 v2).**

- [`findings/open-questions/constructional-monotonicity-addarm-headroom.md`](findings/open-questions/constructional-monotonicity-addarm-headroom.md) — status: **answered** (2026-06-28; created s132, answered s133); a design-level feasibility page responding to the **s132 KEEP-OPEN** review of [`decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization`](decisions/resolved/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-operationalization.md). Works the review's **load-bearing blocker** — **undemonstrated add-arm headroom** for the resultative add arm — at the **design level only** (demonstrates nothing; ratifies / freezes / picks nothing). Argues the resultative degeneracy risk (the conjecture's distributionally-cheap mechanism + the **AANN default-coincidence trap** + resultative base accuracy 0.77–0.89 with **no off-ceiling signal** → a ceiling-pinned add arm would make "add easy / cancel hard" a **near-tautology of the arm construction**, an inadvertent path to spurious confirmation); states what a **clean add control** requires (a control **off-ceiling** on the entailment) and a 4-step **frozen-calibration** test described-not-run; surveys candidate add constructions (Scivetti's eight + Levin class + AANN as cautionary precedent) with honest per-candidate headroom verdicts, **picking none**; and proposes provisional **frozen-threshold shapes** (placeholders), quoting the cc-v2 decision's "frozen WITH the item set" to establish they are **item-set-specific, not portable**. **ANSWERED s133:** the calibration this page specified ran → [`result/addarm-headroom-calibration-v1`](findings/results/addarm-headroom-calibration-v1.md) (both candidate add arms demonstrate headroom; resultative degeneracy worry refuted; prerequisite (1) discharged). The result page carries the reciprocal `refines` link. `refines` [`conjecture/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry`](findings/conjectures/constructional-monotonicity-asymmetry.md); `depends-on` [`open-question/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-design`](findings/open-questions/constructional-monotonicity-generalization-design.md) + the conative-cancel-v2 / answer-key / implicit-cue results + coercion / Scivetti resource. (**empirical / constructional track**)
- [`findings/open-questions/grounding-magnitude-instrument.md`](findings/open-questions/grounding-magnitude-instrument.md) — status: **open** (2026-06-28, session 129); a **$0 scoping** question on the **grounding axis**. With the VWSD competence-audited fluent-channel route to the grounding-headroom **magnitude** sub-bet (prediction 3) now **blocked** (the fluent channel reads 0.438 strict referent-recovery, below the [0.60,0.95] floor — [`result/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-regrade-v1`](findings/results/vwsd-grounding-headroom-nlbaseline-regrade-v1.md)), what **different instrument** could test how *wide* the headroom is? Derives four requirements from the block — (a) a text channel whose competence on the *specific target items* can be **certified**, (b) a **graded human signal** (binary VWSD gold is weak for a magnitude), (c) image-native / fine-polysemy material, (d) the **de-referencing trap avoided** — and assesses in-repo candidates against them: **THINGS-data triplets** (graded + multi-rater + images, but a **construct mismatch** — object-similarity ≠ word-sense relatedness — so *scaffolding, not the magnitude anchor*), **VWSD** (blocked), **DWUG** (graded same-word usage pairs but **text-only, no images**), **Usim/WiC** (Usim graded but `external-only` and **not currently fetchable**). Honest bottom line: no candidate yet meets all four; THINGS is the one worth a future $0 deeper scout *as scaffolding only*; **nothing here rescues VWSD** and a re-attempt owes a genuinely new instrument, not a re-run. **s130 deeper open-access scout (update):** widened the hunt — RAW-C/SAW-C, CxC, SID, BabelPic, VisualSem, PiCS, Mooney-THINGS all fail a specific requirement (graded same-word sense relatedness is text-only; graded image signals are object/scene-construct; sense-tagged image sets are binary); THINGS-scaffolding judged buildable-in-principle but **NOT tractable in-house** (the graded sense labels over images need forbidden new annotation); **sharpened bottom line — prediction-3 magnitude is untested and, on current open resources, un-instrumentable; the only route is an externally-released graded-image set.** `depends-on` [`conjecture/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom`](findings/conjectures/distributional-saturation-grounding-headroom.md) + the two VWSD result pages + the assessed resources. (**empirical / grounding track**)

Both **new verbal** cancel directions built for the generalization battery floored B2 (s135 *for*-durative single-occurrence 0.00 structural; C1 telic-completion 0.25/0.375/0.75, 0/3 at ceiling). So a **clean within-verbal generalization confirm** has not been obtained: is a NEW (not the original conative, whose contact default *is* held at 91.7–100%) within-verbal cancel default at ceiling findable at all on this strict-NLI panel, or is the matched within-verbal cancel arm a **near-principled limit** (the panel reads the project's natural new verbal defaults — aspect, quantity — as defeasible-not-categorical)? Derives four requirements (a held verbal entailment at B2 ceiling; a construction that cancels it; genuinely new; no domain smuggling); surveys candidate verbal directions ($0, none run) — conative-adjacent affected-object family most B2-promising (but generalization-vs-re-read risk), implicative-verb entailments plausibly B2-eligible (constructional framing unproven), aspect/quantity closed; binds the do-not-re-grind discipline (s135 for-durative + C1 completion ruled out; frozen add arm + s134 thresholds untouched). Parallel to [`open-question/grounding-magnitude-instrument`](findings/open-questions/grounding-magnitude-instrument.md) (un-instrumentability). `depends-on` the conjecture + the three B2 calibrations + the C2 battery + conative-cancel-v2 + [`essay/nothing-to-cancel`](findings/essays/nothing-to-cancel.md). The per-construction *arms* already have a human comparison ([`result/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1`](findings/results/scivetti-cxnli-answer-key-v1.md)), but the **gap** does not, for three reasons: Scivetti gives a **single binary gold**, not the graded *robustness* signal the asymmetry is measured in ("not per-item graded human inference ratings" — [`resource/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset`](base/resources/scivetti-2025-cxnli-dataset.md)); its items are **not difficulty-matched across arms** (the answer-key add-vs-cancel contrast is "baseline-difficulty-confounded and is not the matched-difficulty test the conjecture requires"); and the project's **actual cancel constructions** (progressive / privative / completion / single-occurrence) are **absent** from Scivetti's 8. Names what would unlock it (an externally-released graded-cancellability human resource over matched categorical/defeasible pairs → trigger (a) of [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) would fire); surfaces-not-dismisses two partial routes (confine-to-arms = already done, not the gap; a neutral-gold-as-defeasance-proxy re-analysis = doubly confounded + needs cross-session-ratified operationalization). Parallel to [`open-question/grounding-magnitude-instrument`](findings/open-questions/grounding-magnitude-instrument.md). Binds a do-not-re-grind discipline. `depends-on` the conjecture + the answer-key result + the Scivetti resource + within-verbal-battery + conative-cancel-v2 + [`essay/construct-validity-without-a-criterion`](findings/essays/construct-validity-without-a-criterion.md) + [`essay/no-admissible-certifier`](findings/essays/no-admissible-certifier.md). - [`findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md`](findings/open-questions/instrument-sensitivity-constructional-inference.md) — status: open (updated 2026-05-31); does measured constructional-inference competence depend on the **elicitation instrument** (NLI vs forced-choice)? Motivated by own-design results where gpt-5.4-mini diverges across instruments. **Now characterized by three results** ([`result/comparative-correlative-covariation-v3`](findings/results/comparative-correlative-covariation-v3.md), [`result/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c`](findings/results/caused-motion-near-miss-v2c.md), [`result/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1`](findings/results/instrument-disagreement-reanalysis-v1.md)): **two sources** of fragility — a model-specific one (gpt-5.4-mini's excluded-middle slip under negation) and a *general* NLI-vs-FC pragmatics/entailment effect (all 3 models) — and the re-analysis bounds its pervasiveness (large disagreement confined to gpt × conative). Stays **open** (no dedicated cross-instrument design run). Gives a typed home to the theory page's "instrument-fragility as a first-class variable"; conditions how every Tier-4 result is read.

## How to extend this file

When you add a typed page, add a one-line entry here in the right section. When you retire one, leave the line and append `— retired YYYY-MM-DD`. Do not delete entries; the audit trail matters.
